Galatians 5 13  Yéen nag bokk yi, Yàlla woo na leen, ngeen nekk i gor. Waaye nag buleen ci sukkandiku, bay topp seen nafsu, waaye dimbaleenteleen ci kaw mbëggeel. 
Galatians 5 14  Ndaxte yoon wépp, ndigal lii a ko tënk: «Nanga bëgg sa moroom, ni nga bëgge sa bopp.» 
Galatians 5 15  Waaye moytuleen! Bu ngeen dee màttante ak a lekkante, dingeen yàqante.    
Galatians 5 16  Li ma leen di wax mooy lii: dundleen ci Xelum Yàlla, kon dungeen topp seen nafsu. 
Galatians 5 17  Ndaxte sunu nafsu am na ay bëgg-bëgg yu mengoowul ak yu Xelum Yàlla. Te Xelum Yàlla itam am na ay bëgg-bëgg yu mengoowul ak yu sunu nafsu. Ñoom ñaar dañoo juuyoo ci bépp fànn, ba tax lépp lu ngeen bëggoon a def, dungeen ko man. 
Galatians 5 18  Waaye bu ngeen toppee Xelum Yàlla, nekkatuleen ci kilifteefu yoon wi.    
Galatians 5 19  Kuy topp sa nafsu, nii ngay jëfe: njaaloo, xalaat yu bon, def i ñaawteef ak say cér, 
Galatians 5 20  xërëm, luxus, noonoo ak xuloo, ñeetaane, xadar, diiroo mbagg, féewaloo ak xaajaloo, 
Galatians 5 21  kiñaan, màndite ak xawaare ak yeneen yu ni mel. Léegi nag maa ngi leen di artu, ni ma ko defe woon: ñiy jëfe noonu duñu am cér ci nguuru Yàlla.    
Galatians 5 22  Waaye li Xelu Yàlla mi di meññ mooy: mbëggeel, mbég, jàmm, muñ, laabiir, mbaax, kóllëre, 
Galatians 5 23  lewetaay ak maandute. Yoon wi terewul yu ni mel. 
Galatians 5 24  Léegi ñi bokk nag ci Yeesu Kirist, daaj nañu seen nafsu ca bant ba, wacc ko fa, moom ak ay xemmemam ak ay bëgg-bëggam. 
Galatians 5 25  Gannaaw nag nu ngi dund léegi ci Xelum Yàlla, kon nanu ko topp. 
Galatians 5 26  Bu nu tiitaru di dëkkante, di iñaanante. 
Galatians 6 1  Bokk yi, ku ñu fekk muy def lu Yàlla bëggul, yéen ñi topp Xelum Yàlla, nangeen ko jubbanti ak xol bu lewet. Waaye nanga sàmm sa bopp, ngir bàkkaar bañ laa fiir, yaw itam. 
Galatians 6 2  Jàppalanteleen, noonu dingeen sàmm yoon wi Kirist tëral. 
Galatians 6 3  Ndaxte kuy naagu te fekk doo dara, dangay nax sa bopp. 
Galatians 6 4  Na ku nekk seetlu ni muy beye sasam. Bu ko defee dina man a naw boppam, tey bañ di diirante mbagg ak ñi ci des. 
Galatians 6 5  Ndaxte ku ci nekk dangaa war a yenu sab yen.    
Galatians 6 6  Kiy jàng kàddug Yàlla war na sédd ki koy jàngal ci alalam jépp.    
Galatians 6 7  Bu leen ci dara nax; kenn du fontoo Yàlla, ndaxte lu waay ji, moom ngay góob. 
Galatians 6 8  Ku ji ngir sa nafsu, dinga góob li sa nafsu meññ, maanaam ag yàqute. Waaye ku ji lu soloo ak Xelum Yàlla, li Xel mi meññ ngay góob, maanaam dund gu dul jeex. 
Galatians 6 9  Bunu tàyyi ci def lu baax, ndaxte bu nu ci sawaree, bu waxtu wi jotee dinanu jariñu. 
Galatians 6 10  Noonu fi ak nu koy man, nanuy defal ñépp lu baax, rawatina nag sunu bokk yi gëm.    
Galatians 6 11  Seetleen araf yu mag yii ma leen bind ci sama loxob bopp!    
Galatians 6 12  Ñiy gistal ci seen yaram, ñooñoo bëgg ngeen xaraf, ngir ragal a daj fitna ci yégle deewu Kirist ca bant ba. 
Galatians 6 13  Kureel gi faaydaal xaraf, ñoom ci seen bopp sax, duñu topp yoon wi. Dañoo bëgg a ngeen xaraf, ba ñu man a bàkku ci seen yaram, yéen. 
Galatians 6 14  Man ci sama wàllu bopp, duma bàkku mukk su dul ci deewu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist, ba ñu ko daajee ca bant ba. Deeyam moo tax ma mel ni ku dee ci yëfi àddina; yëfi àddina dee ci man. 
Galatians 6 15  Xaraf ak bañ a xaraf dara amu ci solo. Li am solo mooy nekk mbindeef mu bees. 
Galatians 6 16  Ñiy topp ndigal lii nag, na Yàlla wàcce jàmm ak yërmande ci ñoom, ak ci Israyilu Yàlla.    
Galatians 6 17  Léegi nag, bu ma kenn lëjalati, ndaxte yor naa ci sama yaram ay leget yuy màndargaal ne, jaamu Yeesu laa.    
Galatians 6 18  Bokk yi, na yiwu Yeesu Kirist sunu Boroom ànd ak seen xel. Amiin.
Ephesians 1 1  Man Pool, ndawul Kirist Yeesu ci coobareg Yàlla, maa leen di bind, yéen gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi te gëm Kirist Yeesu ci dëkku Efes. 
Ephesians 1 2  Na leen Yàlla sunu Baay ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist may yiw ak jàmm.    
Ephesians 1 3  Cant ñeel na Yàlla Baayu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist, mi nu sotti ci sunu bokk ci Kirist lépp luy barkeel ci baatin te nekk ca bérab yu kawe ya. 
Ephesians 1 4  Ndaxte ba àddina sosoogul, tànn na nu ci Kirist, ngir nu man a teew fa kanamam, sell te ñàkk sikk. Ci kaw mbëggeelam
Ephesians 1 5  séddoo na nu lu jiitu, def nu ay doomam jaarale ko ci Yeesu Kirist, ndaxte looloo doon yéene ju rafet, ji mu tëral ci coobareem. 
Ephesians 1 6  Na ndamam jolli ndax yiw wu réy, wi mu nu sotti ci Soppeem bi.    
Ephesians 1 7  Moom jot na nu ak deretam ji ñu tuur, maanaam baal nu sunuy bàkkaar, ci kaw yiw wu yaatu,
Ephesians 1 8  wi mu nu baawaanal. Te Yàlla sol na nu xel mu mat ak dégg,
Ephesians 1 9  ci feeñal nu mbóoti coobareem, dëppook yéeneem ju rafet, ji mu jaarale ci Kirist. 
Ephesians 1 10  Mu tëral ne, bu jamono yi wéyee ba lépp mat, dina dajale lépp ci kilifteefu Kirist, muy ci kaw, muy ci suuf. 
Ephesians 1 11  Te am nanu cér ci moom bu nu Yàlla sédd lu jiitu ci dogalam, moom miy doxal lépp ci ni mu ko àttee ci coobareem. 
Ephesians 1 12  Noonu nuy jollil ndamam, nun ñi jëkk a wékk sunu yaakaar ci Kirist.    
Ephesians 1 13  Te yéen itam, bi ngeen déggee kàddug dëgg gi, di xebaar bu baax, bi leen tegtal yoonu mucc, te ngeen gëm ko, Yàlla tàmpe na leen ni ñoñam ak Xel mu Sell, mi mu dige woon. 
Ephesians 1 14  Te Xel mi mooy dawal gi nu Yàlla jox ci cér, bi mu nu dencal, ba kera muy goreel ñi mu jotal boppam, te ñépp jollil ndamam.    
Ephesians 1 15  Bi ma déggee nag seen ngëm ci Boroom bi Yeesu ak seen mbëggeel ci gaayi Yàlla yu sell yépp, 
Ephesians 1 16  duma noppee sant Yàlla, di leen boole ci samay ñaan. 
Ephesians 1 17  Te li may ñaan Yàllay sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist, di Baay bi yelloo ndam, mooy lii: mu sol leen xel mu xóot, te xamal leen boppam 
Ephesians 1 18  ci leeral seeni xol. Noonu dingeen xam yaakaaru ëllëg, ji leen Yàlla wooye, di ndam lu xel mënta daj, li nekk ci cér, bi mu dencal gaayam yu sell yi. 
Ephesians 1 19  Ngeen xam it, ni kàttanam màgge ba jéggi dayo, jëm ci nun ñi gëm, dëppook dooleem ju ràññiku, 
Ephesians 1 20  ji mu jëfe ci Kirist, ci li mu ko dekkal, dëël ko ci ndeyjooram ca bérab yu kawe ya, 
Ephesians 1 21  mu tiim lu sore malaaka yépp, muy kilifa, boroom sañ-sañ, boroom doole mbaa buur, te gën a màgg wépp tur wu ñu man a tudd, muy tey, muy ëllëg. 
Ephesians 1 22  Yàlla suufeel na lépp fi kanamam, def ko kilifag lépp ci mbooloom ñi gëm, 
Ephesians 1 23  miy jëmmam, di matug Kirist, mi fees mbindeef mu ne ci fànn gu ne. 
Ephesians 2 1  Te yéen itam Yàlla dekkal na leen, yéen ñi doon ndee fa kanamam ci seeni moy ak seeni bàkkaar. 
Ephesians 2 2  Ci biir yooyu ngeen doon dund démb, topp doxalinu àddina, tey déggal kilifag boroom sañ-sañ yi ci jaww ji, di xel mu bon miy jëf ci kureelu ñi déggadil Yàlla. 
Ephesians 2 3  Te nun it booba àndoon nanu ak ñoom ca seen dund ga, di topp sunu bakkan ciy wut bànneexi yaram ak coobarey xel. Noonu ci sunu bindu nit yeyoo nanu meru Yàlla, ni ña ca des. 
Ephesians 2 4  Waaye Yàlla mi bare yërmande, ci kaw mbëggeel gu réy, gi mu am ci nun,
Ephesians 2 5  dundalaat na nu ak Kirist, fekk ndee lanu woon fa kanamam ci sunuy bàkkaar — ci kaw yiwu Yàlla ngeen mucce. 
Ephesians 2 6  Te dekkal na nu ak Kirist Yeesu, dëël nu ak moom ca bérab yu kawe ya. 
Ephesians 2 7  Noonu ba fu jamono yem, dina lañal fi sunu kanam yiwam wu réy wi xel mënta takk, jaar ci baaxaay gi mu nu won ci Kirist Yeesu. 
Ephesians 2 8  Ndaxte ci yiwu Yàlla ngeen mucce ci kaw ngëm, te loolu jógewul ci yéen, mayu Yàlla la;
Ephesians 2 9  du peyu jëf, ngir kenn du ci kañu. 
Ephesians 2 10  Ndaxte jëfu Yàlla lanu; moo nu bind ci Kirist Yeesu, ngir nu wéy ci jëf yu rafet, yi mu nu fàgguloon ca njàlbéen ga.    
Ephesians 2 11  Kon nag yéen ñi dul Yawut cib juddu, yéen ñi xaraful, te ñi xaraf ci seen yaram ci loxol nit ñoo leen teg ay yéefar, fàttalikuleen lii: 
Ephesians 2 12  booba amuleen woon benn cér ci Kirist, mbaa benn baat ci kureelu bànni Israyil. Bokkuleen woon ci kóllëre, gi Yàlla fas ak ñoom, te ëmb dige ya. Amuleen woon jenn yaakaar mbaa benn xam-xamu Yàlla ci àddina. 
Ephesians 2 13  Waaye léegi ci seen bokk ci Kirist Yeesu, yéen ñi sore woon jege ngeen ndax deretu Kirist ji ñu tuur.    
Ephesians 2 14  Ndaxte mooy sunu jàmm, moom mi jël Yawut ak ki dul Yawut, def nu benn. Ñag bi doxoon sunu diggante te sosoon sunu dëngoo, moo ko màbb ci li mu joxe yaramam, 
Ephesians 2 15  far noonu yoonu Musaa, muy ndigal ya ak dogal ya. Noonu la nu jële, Yawut ak ki dul Yawut, def nu benn ci moom, ba nu jàmmoo. 
Ephesians 2 16  Te nun ñaar, ñi def benn jëmm, jubale na nu ak Yàlla ci dee, gi mu dee ca bant ba ñu ko daajoon, dindee noonu sunu tongoonte. 
Ephesians 2 17  Bi mu ko defee mu ñëw, yégalsi nu xebaaru jàmm fa kanam Yàlla, yéen ñi sore woon ak nun ñi jege. 
Ephesians 2 18  Ndaxte nun ñaar ñépp am nanu bunt ci Yàlla Baay bi, jaar ci Kirist, ci ndimbalu menn Xel mu Sell mi.    
Ephesians 2 19  Noonu dootuleen ay doxandéem mbaa ay gan, waaye am ngeen baat ci kureelu gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi, te waa këram ngeen. 
Ephesians 2 20  Yéena ngi sukkandikoo ci fondamaa, bi ndawi Kirist yi ak yonent yi tabax, te Kirist Yeesu ci boppam di doju dalil wa. 
Ephesians 2 21  Ci moom la doj yépp ràbbloo, ba tabax bi jóg, di màggalukaay bu sell ngir Boroom bi. 
Ephesians 2 22  Te ci seen bokk ci Kirist, Yàlla boole na leen tabax yéen itam, ba ngeen nekk dëkkukaayam, jaar ci Xel mu Sell mi.
Ephesians 3 1  Kon nag maa ngi leen di ñaanal, man Pool mi ñu tëj kaso ci turu Kirist ndax sas wi may bey ci yéen, xeet yi dul Yawut. 
Ephesians 3 2  Wóor na ma ne, dégg ngeen yenub xamle yiwu Yàlla, bi mu ma jagleel jëm ci yéen. 
Ephesians 3 3  Yàlla feeñu na ma, xamal ma mbóoti mbir mi mu tëral, ni ma leen ko binde ci kàddu yu néew. 
Ephesians 3 4  Bu ngeen jàngee loolu, dingeen man a xam bu wér dégg, gi ma am ci mbóoti mbiri Kirist. 
Ephesians 3 5  Ci jamono yu weesu, loolu kumpa la woon ci doom Aadama, waaye léegi Yàlla feeñalal na ko ay ndawam ak yonentam yu sell yi, jaarale ko ci Xel mu Sell mi. 
Ephesians 3 6  Mbir mi nii la tëdde: léegi xeet yi dul Yawut dañoo bokksi cér ak Yawut yi, bokk ak ñoom jenn jëmm, bokk wàll ci xéewal yi Yàlla dige ci Kirist Yeesu, te xebaar bu baax bi xamle ko.    
Ephesians 3 7  Xamle xebaar bu baax boobu nag, Yàlla fal na ma ci jawriñ ci kaw yiwam, te di ma dooleel ci kàttanam. 
Ephesians 3 8  May na ma, man mi gën a tuuti ci gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi, may xebaar xeeti àddina barkeel yu xel dajul yi ci Kirist;
Ephesians 3 9  te it may sulli melokaanu mbir mu xóot mi Yàlla tëral, te doon kumpa njàlbéen ga ba tey ci moom, mi sos lépp. 
Ephesians 3 10  Waaye léegi nee na fàŋŋ, ngir kilifa yi ak boroom sañ-sañ yi ca bérab yu kawe ya man a xam ni Xelum Yàlla xóote, jaar ci li ñu gis ci mbooloom ñi gëm Kirist. 
Ephesians 3 11  Mooy dogal bi sax dàkk, te Yàlla tëral ko ci Kirist Yeesu sunu Boroom. 
Ephesians 3 12  Ci turam am nanu kóolute fa kanam Yàlla, ak bunt bu yaatu ci moom ci kaw ngëm. 
Ephesians 3 13  Maa ngi leen di ñaan nag, ngeen bañ a yoqi ndax coono, yi may jële ci bey sama sas ci yéen, xam ne coono yooyu ñoo leen di jural ndam.    
Ephesians 3 14  Moo tax maa ngi sukk, jublu ci Yàlla Baay 
Ephesians 3 15  biy cosaanul njaboot gépp, muy ci kaw, muy ci suuf. 
Ephesians 3 16  Ma di ko ñaan, mu may leen, ci kaw ndamam lu amul kem, Xel mu Sell mi feddali seen baatin ak kàttan gu mag, 
Ephesians 3 17  ba Kirist dëkk ci seeni xol ci kaw ngëm. Te ngeen sax noonu te sampu ci mbëggeelu Yàlla, 
Ephesians 3 18  ba jagoo, yéen ak gaayi Yàlla yu sell yépp, guddaay ba, yaatuwaay ba, kawe ga ak xóotaay ba, 
Ephesians 3 19  te xam mbëggeelu Kirist, gi raw mépp xel. Noonu dingeen fees dell ak matug Yàlla.    
Ephesians 3 20  Léegi nag, na ndam li féete ak Yàlla, mi man a yeggale lépp luy ñaan mbaa yéene, ba weesu ko fuuf, dëppook kàttan giy jëf ci nun; 
Ephesians 3 21  moo yelloo ndamul mbooloom ñi gëm jamonoy jamono ba fàww, jaar ci Kirist Yeesu. Amiin.
Ephesians 4 1  Man mi ñu tëj kaso ngir Boroom bi nag, maa ngi leen di dénk, ngeen dund dundin wu yellook wooteb Yàlla. 
Ephesians 4 2  Ngeen woyof toyy te lewet, di muñalante tey baalante ci mbëggeel,
Ephesians 4 3  te dem ba fu seen kàttan yem, ngeen likkoo ci jàmm, bay sàmm booloo gi leen Xelum Yàlla may.    
Ephesians 4 4  Jenn jëmm moo am, menn Xel, ak jenn yaakaaru ëllëg ju wooteb Yàlla ëmb. 
Ephesians 4 5  Benn Boroom it a am, genn ngëm, ak benn seedeb ngëm ci li ñu leen sóob ci ndox. 
Ephesians 4 6  Te jenn Yàllaa am, di Baayu ñépp, mu tiim ñépp, fees ñépp, te dëkk ci ñépp.    
Ephesians 4 7  Waaye ku nekk ci nun ak mayam, ni nu ko Kirist séddalee. 
Ephesians 4 8  Looloo tax Mbind mi ne:«Yéeg na ba ca fa gën a kawe,yóbbaale mbooloom noon mu bare, mi mu noot,tey séddale nit ñi ay may.»
Ephesians 4 9  Su nu waxee ne «yéeg na,» li moo ci génn: daa jëkk a wàcc ba ca bérab ya gën a suufe. 
Ephesians 4 10  Ki wàccoon moo yéegaat, ba tiim asamaan yépp, ngir fees lépp. 
Ephesians 4 11  Moo may ñii di ay ndawam, ñii ay yonent, ñii ay taskati xebaar bu baax bi, ak ñeneen ñuy sàmm mbooloom ñi gëm te di ko jàngal. 
Ephesians 4 12  Maye na leen, ngir ñu waajal gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi, ñu man a bey seen sas ci taxawal mbooloom Kirist, di jëmmam. 
Ephesians 4 13  Noonu nu mànkoo ci sunu ngëm ak ci xam Doomu Yàlla ji, ba kera nuy egg ci nekk nit ku sotti, te taxaw taxawaay bu dëppook matug Kirist.    
Ephesians 4 14  Noonu dootunu ay gune yu njàngalem nit ku ñëw di fàbbi ci seeni làqarci ak seeni pexe, nu mel ni ay gaal yu duus yi ak ngelaw li di baaje. 
Ephesians 4 15  Waaye dinanu wax dëgg, ëmb ko ci mbëggeel, bay màgg ci fànn gu ne ci sunu bokk ci Kirist. Mooy bopp, 
Ephesians 4 16  te jëmm jépp ci moom lay dunde, di jëmm ju ràbboo te déggoo ci bépp tenqoo, te cér bu nekk di def warugaram. Noonu jëmm ji di yokku ak a màgg ci biir mbëggeel.    
Ephesians 4 17  Maa ngi leen di wax lii nag, te di ko dëggal ci kanamu Boroom bi: buleen dundeeti ni xeeti àddina yi, ci seeni xalaati neen 
Ephesians 4 18  ak seen xel mu lëndëm. Dañoo génn ci dundu Yàlla, ndax umple gi ñu am ci moom, ak li ñu ko tëjal seen xol. 
Ephesians 4 19  Seen xol dafa dërkiis, ba ñu bayliku ciy topp seen nafsu, di sóobu ci bépp sobe te xér ci.    
Ephesians 4 20  Waaye du dundin woowu ngeen jàng ci Kirist. 
Ephesians 4 21  Ndax yaakaar naa ne, dégg ngeen Kirist te jàng ngeen ci moom, ba xam dëgg gi Yeesu ëmb. 
Ephesians 4 22  Maanaam ngeen yulli seen jikko ju bon, ji ngeen judduwaale te daan fés ci seeni jëf, te muy gën a yées, moom ak i bëgg-bëggam yuy naxe kese. 
Ephesians 4 23  Te ngeen yeeslu ci seen biir xel, 
Ephesians 4 24  te soloo jikko ju bees, ji Yàlla sàkk ci njub ak sell yu dëggu.    
Ephesians 4 25  Kon nag bàyyileen di fen, tey wax dëgg kenn ku nekk ci moroomam, ndax ku nekk sa genn-wàllu moroom nga. 
Ephesians 4 26  Ku mer, bu mu jàll aw kaañ; bu jant bi sowaale seen mer, 
Ephesians 4 27  ba ngeen may Seytaane bunt. 
Ephesians 4 28  Ku daan sàcc, na ko dëddu te jublu ci liggéey lu baax ci ay loxoom, ngir mu man a dimbali ñi néew doole.    
Ephesians 4 29  Bu genn kàddu gu ñaaw génn ci seen gémmiñ, waaye su wax yegsee, nangeen wax lu rafet, ba faj soxlay seeni moroom, te teg ñi leen di déglu ci yoonu yiw. 
Ephesians 4 30  Buleen yóbbe tiis Xelu Yàlla mu Sell, mi leen tàmpe ngir bésu goreel ba. 
Ephesians 4 31  Dëdduleen lépp luy wex mbaa tàng bopp, luy mer mbaa coow, lépp luy xaste mbaa coxor. 
Ephesians 4 32  Te ngeen baax ci seen diggante, di laayante biir tey baalante, ni leen Yàlla baale ci turu Kirist.
Ephesians 5 1  Yéen nag ñiy guney Yàlla, yi mu bëgg ci xolam, royleen ko ci loolu. 
Ephesians 5 2  Ngeen wéer seen dund ci mbëggeel, mel ni Kirist mi nu bëgg, ba joxe bakkanam ngir nun, di sarax su ñu jébbal Yàlla te neex ko ni xetu latkoloñ.    
Ephesians 5 3  Waaye naka njaaloo ak bépp sobe mbaa bëgge, jéllale naa jëf ji sax, waaye bu ko làmmiñ tudd, ni mu jekke ci gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi. 
Ephesians 5 4  Dawleen it yu jekkadee, ni wax ju ñaaw mbaa waxi caaxaan ak kaf yu bon, te ngeen sax ci sant Yàlla. 
Ephesians 5 5  Na leen wóor ne, kenn ku jikkowoo ndoxaan, sobe mbaa bëgge, maanaam bokkaale Yàlla, kooku du am cér ci nguuru Kirist ak Yàlla. 
Ephesians 5 6  Bu leen kenn nax ci ay waxi neen, ndaxte jëf yooyooy tax meru Yàlla di wàcc ci kureelu ñi ko déggadil. 
Ephesians 5 7  Kon nag buleen séq ak ñoom dara. 
Ephesians 5 8  Lëndëm ngeen woon, waaye léegi leer ngeen ndax seen bokk ci Boroom bi. Dundeleen nag ni ay guney leer. 
Ephesians 5 9  Leer, mbaax lay meññ, njub ak dëgg. 
Ephesians 5 10  Dëggal-leen ci seeni jëf li neex Boroom bi, 
Ephesians 5 11  te daw lépp luy jëfi lëndëm yu amul njariñ, bay weer sax ku koy def. 
Ephesians 5 12  Ndaxte waxtaane sax li ñuy def ci nëbbu, lu ruslu la; 
Ephesians 5 13  waaye leer, lu mu ëmb, fésal ko. 
Ephesians 5 14  Ndaxte lu jaxasoo ak leer di leer. Looloo tax ñu ne:«Yeewul, yaw mi nelaw,te jóge ci biir néew yi,kon Kirist dina ne ràññ ci yaw,ni leeru jant buy fenk.»    
Ephesians 5 15  Noonu sàmmleen seen dundin, waxuma ni ñu amul xel, waaye ni ñu am xel, 
Ephesians 5 16  tey jariñoo jot gi, ndaxte nu ngi ci jamono ju bon. 
Ephesians 5 17  Buleen ñàkk bopp nag, waaye xamleen liy coobareg Boroom bi. 
Ephesians 5 18  Buleen màndi it ci sangara, liy ndeyi ñaawteef, waaye feesleen ak Xel mu Sell mi; 
Ephesians 5 19  di waxante ci seen biir ci ay taalifi Sabóor, ci ay woy ak ay cant yu tukkee ci Xelum Yàlla, di woy ak a kañ Boroom bi ci seeni xol. 
Ephesians 5 20  Gërëmleen Yàlla Baay bi ci turu Yeesu Kirist Boroom bi, fu ngeen man a tollu, ci lu mu man a doon; 
Ephesians 5 21  teg ca nangul sa moroom ci biir wegeelu Kirist.    
Ephesians 5 22  Naka yéen jigéen ñi, nangeen nangul seeni jëkkër, ni su doon Boroom bi. 
Ephesians 5 23  Ndaxte góor mooy kilifag jabaram, ni Kirist nekke kilifag mbooloom ñi gëm, muy jëmmam ji muy sàmm. 
Ephesians 5 24  Ni mbooloo mi nag jiitale Kirist, noonu la jigéen ji war a jiitale jëkkëram ci lépp.    
Ephesians 5 25  Yéen nag góor ñi, na ku nekk bëgg jabaram, ni Kirist bëgge mbooloo mi, ba joxe bakkanam ndax moom, 
Ephesians 5 26  ngir sellal ko ak kàddoom, ba mu laab ni ku sangu set. 
Ephesians 5 27  Noonu dina ko jël, mu mel ni séet bu ñu waajal, di mbooloom mu soloo ndam, te gàkkul, rasul, taqul leneen, waaye mu sell te amul sikk.    
Ephesians 5 28  Na góor bëgg jabaram, ni mu bëgge boppam. Bëgg sa jabar, bëgg sa bopp la. 
Ephesians 5 29  Ndaxte kenn musul a bañ sa yaram. Waaye danga koy dundal, di ko fonk. Noonu it la Kirist fonke mbooloo mi; 
Ephesians 5 30  ndaxte noo di céri jëmmam. 
Ephesians 5 31  Mbind mi nee na: «Moo tax góor dina beru ndeyam ak baayam, di taq ci jabaram, ñoom ñaar doon benn.» 
Ephesians 5 32  Loolu ëmb na mbóot mu xóot; man maa ngi wax ci lu jëm ci Kirist ak mbooloo mi. 
Ephesians 5 33  Waaye li teew, na góor gu nekk bëgg jabaram, ni mu bëgge boppam, te jigéen ji weg jëkkëram.
Ephesians 6 1  Naka yéen xale yi, nangeen déggal seeni waajur, ci li ngeen bokk ci Boroom bi, ndaxte looloo rafet. 
Ephesians 6 2  «Teralal sa ndey ak sa baay,» mooy ndigal li jëkk a ëmb dige,
Ephesians 6 3  maanaa: «ngir nga am gudd fan gu ànd ak jàmm.»    
Ephesians 6 4  Yéen baay yi it, buleen bundaxataal xale yi, waaye ngeen yar leen, di leen yemale ak a yee ci Boroom bi.    
Ephesians 6 5  Yéen jaam yi, nangeen déggal seeni sang yu àddina, boole ci ragal ak wegeel, di ko def ak xol bu laab, ni su doon ngir Kirist. 
Ephesians 6 6  Buleen ko def rekk ci ngistal, ngir sàkku ngërëmu nit, waaye ni ay jaami Kirist, di jëfe coobareg Yàlla ak seen xol bépp. 
Ephesians 6 7  Beyleen seen sas nag ak xol bu tàlli, ni su doon ngir Boroom bi te du nit,
Ephesians 6 8  xam ne ku def lu baax, Boroom bi delloo la ko, muy jaam, muy gor.    
Ephesians 6 9  Yéen it sang yi, jëfeleen noonu seen diggante ak seeni jaam, te dëddu gépp raglu, xam ne yéena bokk benn Boroom ci asamaan, te ñépp a yem fi moom.    
Ephesians 6 10  Léegi nag doolewuleen ci Boroom bi, te soloo kàttanam gu mag gi. 
Ephesians 6 11  Gànnaayooleen yérey xarey Yàlla yépp, ngir man a jànkoonte ak pexey Seytaane. 
Ephesians 6 12  Ndaxte ndëndu xare jib na, waxuma sunu diggante ak nit ñi, waaye ak kilifa yiy nëxal àddina si, ñuy kilifa yi ak ay boroom sañ-sañ, di gaayi Seytaane yi ci bérab yu kawe yi. 
Ephesians 6 13  Kon nag gànnaayooleen yérey xarey Yàlla yépp, ba man a jànkoonte jamono ju xeex bi taree, noot lépp te taxaw temm.    
Ephesians 6 14  Taxawleen kon temm, geñoo dëgg te sàngoo njub, muy seen kiiraayu dënn. 
Ephesians 6 15  Solooleen jàmm, ji xebaar bu baax biy joxe, ni ay dàll ci seeni tànk, ba jekk ci lépp. 
Ephesians 6 16  Defleen it ngëm, muy seen pakk, ba man a fél jum yi leen Seytaane di fitt. 
Ephesians 6 17  Defleen mucc, muy seen mbaxanam xare, ak kàddug Yàlla, muy jaasi ji leen Xel mu Sell mi tëggal. 
Ephesians 6 18  Deeleen ñaan ci xeeti ñaan yépp ci kàttanu Xel mu Sell mi, te sax ci ak farlu gu mat sëkk, di ñaanal gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi yépp.    
Ephesians 6 19  Te buleen ma ci fàtte, ngir waxtu wu ma ubbee sama gémmiñ, ma am lu ma wax, ba man a xamle ak fit wu dëgër mbóoti xebaar bu baax bi. 
Ephesians 6 20  Ndaw laa ci, lu ñu jéng; na ma Yàlla may fit wu ma waxe, ni mu ma ware.    
Ephesians 6 21  Yónnee naa leen Tisig sama mbokk, mi ma sopp, te muy jawriñ ju takku ci liggéeyu Boroom bi, ngir mu xamal leen lépp li aju ci man ak li may def. 
Ephesians 6 22  Maa leen ko yónneel sama bopp, ngir ngeen xam li nu nekke, te mu dëfël seeni xol.    
Ephesians 6 23  Yéen bokk yi, na leen Yàlla Baay bi ak Yeesu Kirist Boroom bi may jàmm ak mbëggeel gu ànd ak ngëm. 
Ephesians 6 24  Na yiwu Yàlla ànd ak ñépp, ñi bëgg Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist ak mbëggeel gu sax.
Philippians 1 1  Nun Pool ak Timote, jaami Kirist Yeesu, noo leen di bind, yéen gaayi Yàlla yu sell yépp ci dëkku Filib, yi bokk ci Kirist Yeesu, yéen ak seeni njiit ak ñiy topptoo yëfi mbooloo mi. 
Philippians 1 2  Na leen Yàlla sunu Baay ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist may yiw ak jàmm.    
Philippians 1 3  Yoon wu ma leen di xalaat, maa ngi sant Yàlla sama Boroom;
Philippians 1 4  te saa su ma leen di ñaanal yéen yépp, duma noppee bég,
Philippians 1 5  ndax seen ànd ak man ci tas xebaar bu baax bi, ca ndoorte la ba tey. 
Philippians 1 6  Wóor na ma ne, Yàlla mi tàmbali jëf ju baax jii ci yéen, dina ci sax, ba bésu Kirist Yeesu ñëw.    
Philippians 1 7  Te juumuma ci li ma xalaat loolu ci yéen ñépp, ndaxte def naa leen ci sama xol; ba tax fii ci kaso bi, ci taxawal xebaar bu baax bi ak lawal ko, yéen ñépp am ngeen wàll ak man ci yiwu Yàlla. 
Philippians 1 8  Ndaxte Yàllaa seede ne, sama xol seey na ci yéen ñépp ci biir cofeelu Kirist Yeesu.    
Philippians 1 9  Li ma leen di ñaanal nag mooy lii: na seen mbëggeel di yokku tey gën a tar, jaar ci xam ak xàmmi gu wér; 
Philippians 1 10  nangeen sax noonu ci yi gën a rafet, ngeen am xol bu laab te bañ a am benn sikk, ba bésu Kirist ñëw; 
Philippians 1 11  na seen xol meññ njub, ba ne gàññ, jaar ci Yeesu Kirist ci ndamul Yàlla ak cantam.    
Philippians 1 12  Damaa bëgg, bokk yi, ngeen xam lii: li ma dal taxul xebaar bu baax dellu gannaaw, waaye da koo jëmale kanam. 
Philippians 1 13  Noonu ñiy wottu buur bi ak ñépp gis nañu bu leer ne, turu Kirist rekk a tax ñu jàpp ma. 
Philippians 1 14  Te it bokk yu bare takk nañu seeni fit ci li ñu gis samay buum, ba tax ñu gën a ñeme ci wax kàddug Yàlla ci lu àndul ak genn tiit.    
Philippians 1 15  Am na ñuy waare ci turu Kirist ci kaw kiñaan ak xëccoo, waaye ñi ci des ci kaw cofeel ak xol bu laab, ndaxte xam nañu ne, Yàlla moo ma teg fii, ngir ma taxawal xebaar bu baax bi. 
Philippians 1 16  Waaye ñale amuñu xol bu laab, te seen njariñu bopp rekk a tax ñuy yégle turu Kirist, di wut a feddali samay buum ak coono.    
Philippians 1 17  Lu ci génn nag? Xanaa lii rekk: turu Kirist jolli na ci nii mbaa naa, muy ci naaféq, muy ci dëgg; bég naa ci te dinaa ci bégati. 
Philippians 1 18  Ndaxte xam naa ne, loolu lépp mu ngi jëm ci sama mucc, jaar ci seeni ñaan ak ndimbalu Xelum Yeesu Kirist, mi ma Yàllay yéwénal. 
Philippians 1 19  Ndaxte sama xënte ak sama yaakaar mooy ma bañ a rus ci lenn, waaye sama yaram feeñal ndamu Kirist, ma ànd ci ak kóolute gu mat, su may dund mbaa may dee; moom laa daan def démb, te moom laay def tey. 
Philippians 1 20  Ndaxte su ma dundee, Kirist laay noyyee, te su ma deeyee, xéewal lay doon ci man. 
Philippians 1 21  Su ma Yàlla bàyyee ci àddina, sas wu am njariñ la ci man. Am naa xel ñaar, te xawma bi ci gën. Am naa yéeney jóge fi, fekki Kirist, te looloo gën fuuf, 
Philippians 1 22  waaye ma des fi ci àddina moo gën ci yéen. 
Philippians 1 23  Loolu wóor na ma; kon xam naa ne, dinaa fi des, di leen taxawu yéen ñépp, ngir seen ngëm yokku, ànd ak mbég. 
Philippians 1 24  Noonu dinaa dellusi ci yéen, ngir sama taxawaay gën a lawal seen mbég ci Kirist Yeesu.    
Philippians 1 25  Waaye dénk naa leen lii: na seeni jëf yelloo ak li Kirist digle ci xebaar bu baax bi. Noonu su ma leen seetsee, mbaa ma dégg seen mbir rekk, dinaa xam ne yéena ngi dëgër ci menn xel, bokk benn xalaat ci bëre luy saxal dëggu xebaar bu baax bi, 
Philippians 1 26  te bañ a tiit dara ndax noon, yi leen di xëbal. Màndarga la muy wone ne aji sànku lañu, di màndarga it ne aji mucc ngeen, di mucc gu jóge ci Yàlla. 
Philippians 1 27  Ndaxte Yàlla may na leen, ngeen gëm Kirist, rax-ca-dolli ngeen sonn ndax turam, 
Philippians 1 28  di wéy ci bëre, bi ngeen gisoon ci man, te dégg léegi sama mbir.
Philippians 2 1  Su nu Kirist mayee fit nag ak mbëggeel guy dëfël sunu xol, su nu amee cér ci Xel mu Sell mi, su amee cofeel ak yërmande ci sunu bokk ci moom,
Philippians 2 2  kon mottalileen sama mbég, ci bokk benn xalaat ak genn mbëggeel, benn bakkan ak menn xel. 
Philippians 2 3  Buleen def dara ci kaw wut aw tur walla wonu, waaye jiital-leen seeni moroom cig woyof. 
Philippians 2 4  Buleen yem ci topptoo seen bopp rekk, waaye booleleen ci seeni moroom. 
Philippians 2 5  Te ngeen soloo xel mi nekkoon ci Kirist Yeesu:
Philippians 2 6  Njàlbéen ga fekk na Kirist yor melow Yàlla,waaye aakimowul taxawaayamci li mu mengoo ak Yàlla.
Philippians 2 7  Waaye daa wàcce boppam,ba tollook nit ñi,def boppam surga.Te bi mu yoree bindu nit,
Philippians 2 8  daa suufeel boppam,di dégg ndigal, ba joxe boppam,ñu daaj ko sax ci bant.
Philippians 2 9  Moo tax Yàlla kaweel ko lool,jox ko tur wi tiim yépp, 
Philippians 2 10  ngir turu Yeesoo tax ñépp sukk,ci asamaan, ci kaw suuf, ci biir suuf; 
Philippians 2 11  te ñépp bokk genn kàddu naan:Yeesu Kirist mooy Boroom bi;ci màggug Yàlla Baay bi.    
Philippians 2 12  Noonu samay soppe, xam naa ne, musuleen a jóg ci dégg ndigal, waxuma sax bi ma nekkee ak yéen rekk, waaye rawatina bi ma leen soree. Kon nag maa ngi leen di ñaan, ngeen biral seen mucc ci seeni jëf, te def ko ci ragal Yàlla gu dëggu. 
Philippians 2 13  Ndaxte Yàlla ci boppam mooy jëf ci yéen, ngir ngeen fonk coobareem te di ko jëfe.    
Philippians 2 14  Lépp lu ngeen di def nag, buleen ci boole xultu mbaa xuloo. 
Philippians 2 15  Noonu dingeen am xol bu laab bu àndul ak ŋàññ, di guney Yàlla yu amul sikk ci biir jamono ju yàqu te rëb. Dangeen di leer ci seen biir ni weer ci àddina si, 
Philippians 2 16  di jottali kàddug dund gi. Noonu bu bésu Kirist ñëwee, dinaa man a bég, xam ne dawuma lu amul njariñ, te sonnuma cig neen. 
Philippians 2 17  Te bu sama deret waree tuuru sax, ngir seen ngëm mat sëkk, ma mel ni naan gu ñu boole ak sarax su jëm ci Yàlla, ba tey bég naa ci, te dinaa ci bégati. 
Philippians 2 18  Yéen itam nag bégleen, waaw fekksileen ma ci sama mbég.    
Philippians 2 19  Gannaaw loolu, bu soobee Boroom bi Yeesu, yaakaar naa ne, dinaa leen yónnee Timote balaa yàgg, ngir sama xel dal ci xam nan ngeen def. 
Philippians 2 20  Ndaxte amu fi kenn gannaaw Timote, ku bokk ak man xalaat te fonk leen bu wér. 
Philippians 2 21  Ñi ci des ñépp, seen bopp lañuy xalaat, waaye du mbiri Yeesu Kirist. 
Philippians 2 22  Waaye xam ngeen takkuteg Timote, ci ni mu ànde ak man ci tas xebaar bu baax bi, ni doom di taxawoo baayam. 
Philippians 2 23  Moom laa yaakaar a yónni fi yéen nag, waxtu wu ma yégee, nu sama mbir di tëdde. 
Philippians 2 24  Waaye wóor na ma ne, Boroom bi dina ma may, man ci sama bopp, ma seetsi leen balaa yàgg.    
Philippians 2 25  Ci lu jëm ci sama mbokk Epafrodit nag, miy sama nawle ci liggéey bi ak ci xeex bi, te di seen ndaw ci faj samay soxla, jàpp naa ne, war naa leen koo delloo. 
Philippians 2 26  Ndaxte namm na leen lool, te tiisoo na li ngeen yég jagadeem. 
Philippians 2 27  Ci dëgg-dëgg woppoon na ba xaw a dee, waaye Yàlla yërëm na ko, ba fëgg boppam, rax-ca-dolli siggil na ma man itam, ngir ma bañ a am tiis ci kaw tiis. 
Philippians 2 28  Noonu delloo naa leen ko ci lu gaaw, ngir ñëwam bégal seeni xol, te man itam sama xol féex. 
Philippians 2 29  Teeruleen ko teeru bu rafet nag ngir Boroom bi, te teral ñi mel ni moom. 
Philippians 2 30  Ndaxte liggéeyal na Kirist, ba riisu dee, te gar na bakkanam ci taxawal leen ci topptoo, bi ngeen yéene woon ci man.
Philippians 3 1  Kon nag samay bokk, bégleen ci Boroom bi. Duma sonn mukk ci di leen ko wax, ndax seen mucc moo ci aju.    
Philippians 3 2  Moytuleen xaj yi, waaw moytuleen ñiy jëfe lu bon, ñoom ñi seen xarafal weesul wàññi yaramu nit. 
Philippians 3 3  Ndaxte nun noo xaraf tigi, nun ñiy màggal Yàlla ci Xel mu Sell mi, di damu ci Kirist Yeesu, te amunu jenn yaakaar ci matug nit.    
Philippians 3 4  Ba tey manoon naa am yaakaar ci sama bopp; su nit doon damu, maa ciy raw. 
Philippians 3 5  Xarafoon naa ca ayu-bés ga, bokk ci bànni Israyil ci giiru Ben-yamin, di Ibrë ci deret ak ci meen. Bu dee ci yoonu Musaa ngeen bëgg a wax, ci tariixab Farisen laa bokkoon;
Philippians 3 6  bu dee it ci mbirum farlu, daan naa fitnaal mbooloom ñi gëm Kirist; bu dee ci njub ci sàmm yoon, awma benn gàkk.    
Philippians 3 7  Waaye loolu lépp lu ma tegoon ay njariñ fa kanam Yàlla, dëddu naa ko ngir Kirist. 
Philippians 3 8  Rax-ca-dolli dëddu naa lépp ngir xéewali xam Kirist Yeesu sama Boroom, di xam-xam bu xóot, ba xel mënu koo takk. Moo tax ñàkk naa sama lépp, te def ko ni mbalit, ngir am cér ci Kirist. 
Philippians 3 9  Na ma Yàlla fekk ci moom, waxuma ci njub gu aju ci sàmm yoon, waaye gu aju ci gëm Kirist, maanaam njub gi nu Yàlla sol ci kaw ngëm. 
Philippians 3 10  Moom laay ittewoo xam, ak doole ji ànd ak ndekkiteem, ma bokk ci ay coonoom, ba fekki ko ci deeyam, 
Philippians 3 11  ngir man a séddu ci ndekkiteem, su ma ko manee am.    
Philippians 3 12  Waxuma ne jagoo naa ko ba noppi, waxuma it ne aji mat laa, waaye maa ngi daw, ngir jot li tax Kirist jël ma. 
Philippians 3 13  Bokk yi, gëmuma ne jot naa ko ba noppi, waaye lenn lii laay def: fàtte li ma weesu, jublu ci li féete kanam, 
Philippians 3 14  di daw yen muj ga, ngir jot li ma Yàlla tax a woo, di cér bi ma Yàlla wooye te dencal ma ko ci asamaan ci darajay Kirist Yeesu.    
Philippians 3 15  Nun ñi mat nag, nanu xalaat loolu. Te su ngeen ci amee werantey xol, Yàlla dina leen ko leeralal. 
Philippians 3 16  Li am daal, fa seen ngëm tolloo, na fa seen jëf àgg.    
Philippians 3 17  Kon nag bokk yi, toppleen ma te xool ñiy roy ci li nu tëral diirub sunu ngan ci yéen. 
Philippians 3 18  Ndaxte jëfi ñu bare juuyoo na ak dee gi Kirist dee; loolu wax naa leen ko ba tàyyi, maa ngi koy waxaat léegi ak i jooy. 
Philippians 3 19  Alku lañuy mujje, ñoom ñiy jaami seen biir, di wonoo lu ruslu, tey wut yëfi àddina rekk. 
Philippians 3 20  Waaye nun waa asamaan lanu, te noo ngi xaar Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist jóge fa, musalsi nu. 
Philippians 3 21  Noonu dina soppi sunu yaram wu toroxlu, def ko ni yaramam wi ànd ak ndam dëppook kàttanam, gi ko man a nootal mbindeef yépp.
Philippians 4 1  Kon nag yéen samay bokk, ñi ma bëgg te namm leen, di sama mbég ak sama kaalag ndam, jàppleen bu dëgër noonu ci Boroom bi, soppe yi!    
Philippians 4 2  Ci lu jëm ci Ewodi ak Santis, maa ngi leen di ñaan, ñu bokk benn xalaat ci Boroom bi. 
Philippians 4 3  Te yaw sama nawle bu wér, nanga dimbali jigéen ñooñu xeexoon ci sama wet ci tas xebaar bu baax bi, boole ci Këlemaŋ ak samay yeneeni nawle, ñoom ñi Yàlla bind seeni tur ci téereb dund ba.    
Philippians 4 4  Deeleen bég ci Boroom bi; maa ngi koy waxati: bégleen!
Philippians 4 5  Na seen lewet leer ñépp. Boroom bi jege na. 
Philippians 4 6  Buleen jaaxle ci dara, waaye ci lépp wéetal-leen Yàlla, diis ko seeni soxla ci ñaan gu ànd ak cant. 
Philippians 4 7  Noonu jàmmu Yàlla, ji xel mënta takk, dina aar seeni xol ak seeni xalaat ci darajay Kirist Yeesu.    
Philippians 4 8  Léegi nag bokk yi, na seen xalaat jublu ci lii: lu dëggu, lu jekk, lu jub, lu sell, lu rafet ak lu faaydawu; su fi amee lu baax mbaa lu mat a naw, xalaatleen ko. 
Philippians 4 9  Li ngeen jànge ci man te nangu ko, li ngeen dégge ci man te gis ko, jëfeleen ko; kon Yàllay jàmm dina ànd ak yéen.    
Philippians 4 10  Sama xol sedd na guyy ci Boroom bi, ci ni ngeen yeesale seen ndimbal ci man. Xam naa ne, amoon ngeen yéene ji, waaye man gi moo fi nekkul woon. 
Philippians 4 11  Ba tey soxla taxul ma waxe nii, ndaxte jàng naa doylu ci mbir mu ma man a dab. 
Philippians 4 12  Miin naa ñàkk, man naa naataange. Ci fépp ak ci lépp, Yàlla def na ba sama xol toj ci suur ak xiif, barele ak néewle. 
Philippians 4 13  Man naa lépp ci ndimbalu Aji Dooleel ji. 
Philippians 4 14  Waaye teewul taxawu, bi ngeen ma taxawu ci sama tiis, jëf ju rafet la.    
Philippians 4 15  Yéen waa Filib xam ngeen ne, bi ngeen jëkkee xam xebaar bu baax bi, te ma jóge diiwaanu Maseduwan, benn mbooloo àndul woon ak man ci mbirum joqleente ndimbal, mu dul yéen doŋŋ. 
Philippians 4 16  Ba ma nekkee dëkku Tesalonig sax, yónnee ngeen ay yooni yoon, ngir faj samay soxla. 
Philippians 4 17  Loolu tekkiwul ne, damay sàkku ay ndimbal ci yéen, waaye damaa bëgg rekk seen denc yokku fa Yàlla. 
Philippians 4 18  Fi mu ne jot naa li ma aajowoo lépp, ba maa ngi ci naataange; li ngeen ma yónnee ci loxoy Epafrodit doy na sëkk; ni xetu latkoloñ la mel ci man, di sarax su neex Yàlla te mu nangu ko. 
Philippians 4 19  Te Yàlla sama Boroom, mi denc ci Kirist Yeesu xéewal yu dul jeex, dina ci faj seeni soxla yépp.    
Philippians 4 20  Na Yàlla sunu Baay yelloo ndam ba fàww. Amiin.    
Philippians 4 21  Nuyul-leen ma gaayi Kirist Yeesu yu sell yépp. Bokk yi ànd ak man, ñu ngi leen di nuyu. 
Philippians 4 22  Te it gaayi Yàlla yu sell yépp ñu ngi leen di nuyu, rawatina nag ñi nekk kër buur bi Sesaar.    
Philippians 4 23  Na yiwu Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist ànd ak seen xel.
Colossians 1 1  Man Pool, ndawul Kirist Yeesu ci coobareg Yàlla, man ak Timote sunu mbokk,
Colossians 1 2  noo leen di bind, yéen gaayi Yàlla yu sell, yi dëkk Kolos te di ay bokk ci gëm Kirist. Na leen Yàlla sunu Baay may yiw ak jàmm.    
Colossians 1 3  Dunu noppee sant Yàlla, Baayu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist, saa su nu leen di ñaanal,
Colossians 1 4  ndaxte yég nanu seen ngëm ci Kirist Yeesu ak seen mbëggeel ci gaayi Yàlla yépp. 
Colossians 1 5  Ngëm googu ak mbëggeel googu ñu ngi sosoo ci yaakaaru ëllëg, jiy cér bi leen Yàlla dencal ca asamaan. Mas ngeen a dégg yaakaar jooju ci kàddug dëgg gi, di xebaar bu baax bi. 
Colossians 1 6  Ni xebaar bu baax bi wàcce ci yéen, noonu lay wàcce ci àddina sépp, di meññ te di law. Te noonu lay doxale ci yéen, li dale ci bés, ba ngeen dégge xebaaru yiwu Yàlla, te xam dëggam gi mu ëmb;
Colossians 1 7  moom ngeen jànge ci Epafras, miy sunu nawle ci liggéey bi te nu sopp ko, di jawriñu Kirist bu takku ngir seen njariñ. 
Colossians 1 8  Te moo nu yégal it mbëggeel, gi Xelu Yàlla mi sol ci yéen.    
Colossians 1 9  Looloo tax ci sunu wàllu bopp, ba nu ko yégee ba tey, jógunu ci di leen ñaanal. Nu ngi ñaan Yàlla, ngeen xam bu baax coobareem ci xel mu mat ak ràññee gu aju ci dooley Xelam. 
Colossians 1 10  Noonu dingeen dund dund gu dëppoo ak seen bokk ci Boroom bi, ba neex ko ci fànn gu nekk, di def bépp jëf yu baax, te yokk seen xam-xam ci Yàlla. 
Colossians 1 11  Te Yàlla dina leen dooleel ak bépp doole, mu mengoo ak kàttanu ndamam, ngir ngeen man a tegoo coono te muñ, ba fa muñ di yem. 
Colossians 1 12  Dingeen gërëm Yàlla Baay bi, ànd ci ak mbég, moom mi leen jagleel, ngeen bokk ci cér, bi mu dencal gaayam yu sell yi ci leer.    
Colossians 1 13  Yàlla musal na nu ci dooley lëndëm, yóbbu nu ci nguuru Doomam ji mu bëgg, 
Colossians 1 14  moom mi nu jot, maanaam baal nu sunuy bàkkaar.    
Colossians 1 15  Doom jooju moo di melokaanu Yàlla, ji kenn gisul. Mooy taaw bi, ki gën a màgg lépp luy mbindeef. 
Colossians 1 16  Ndaxte ci moom la Yàlla sàkke lépp lu nekk ci asamaan ak suuf, li ñuy gis ak li ñu mënul a gis, muy buur, njiit, kilifa mbaa boroom sañ-sañ. Lépp lu ñu sàkk, ci moom lañu ko jaarale, ci moom lañu ko jëme. 
Colossians 1 17  Laata dara di am, fekkoon na moom mu nekk, te lépp a ngi jàppoo ci moom.    
Colossians 1 18  Mooy bopp bi yilif jëmm ji, di mbooloom ñi ko gëm, ndaxte moom mooy njàlbéen gi, di taaw bi, maanaam ki jëkk a dekki, ngir muy kilifa ci bépp fànn. 
Colossians 1 19  Ndaxte soob na Yàlla mu dëkkal matam gépp ci moom 
Colossians 1 20  te jaar ci moom, jubale lépp ak boppam, muy ci kaw asamaan yi mbaa ci suuf, ba mu wàccee jàmm jaarale ko ci deret ji tuuru, bi Doom ji deeyee ca bant ba.    
Colossians 1 21  Te yéen ñi sore woon Yàlla te doon ay noonam ci seen xel ak seen jëf yu bon, 
Colossians 1 22  léegi nag Yàlla jubale na leen ak boppam jaare ko ci deewu Kirist ci yaramu nitam, ngir taxawal leen ca kanamam, ngeen sell te ñàkk sikk ak i ŋàññ. 
Colossians 1 23  Loolu nag na fekk ngeen wéy ci ngëm, sampu ci ba dëgër ci, tey séentu cér, bi leen xebaar bu baax bi jox. Te xebaar bu baax, boobu ngeen dégg te ñu yégal waa àddina sépp, man Pool moom laay yégle.    
Colossians 1 24  Léegi nag maa ngi am bànneex ci coono, yi may daj ngir seen njariñ; te li des sax ci fitnay Kirist, noonu laa koy àggalee ngir njariñu mbooloom ñi gëm, di jëmmam. 
Colossians 1 25  Jawriñu mbooloo moomu laa, ndaxte Yàlla sas na ma ngir yéen, may yégle fu nekk kàddoom, 
Colossians 1 26  maanaam ma yégle kumpa, gi nëbbu woon ay jamonoy jamono, waaye léegi Yàlla xamal na ko ay gaayam 
Colossians 1 27  ci xeeti àddina sépp. Ñoom nag la Yàlla bëgg a xamal ni ndamu kumpa googu màgge, maanaam Kirist a ngi dëkk ci yéen, di yaakaar ju wér ci ndamu ëllëg.    
Colossians 1 28  Moom Kirist lanuy yégle, di artu te di jàngal ku nekk, ànd ak xel mu mat, ngir jébbal Yàlla ku nekk ni ku mat ci Kirist. 
Colossians 1 29  Ci loolu laay jëmale sama liggéey, di bëree dooley Kirist, jiy yengu ci man ak kàttan.
Colossians 2 1  Bëgg naa nag, ngeen xam bëre bu metti, bi may bëre ngir yéen, ngir waa Lawdise ak ñépp ñi ma musul a teg bët. Damay def sama kem-kàttan,
Colossians 2 2  ngir ngeen am fit te nekk benn ci mbëggeel, ngir dajal noonu xam-xam bu mat, ba xam kumpag Yàlla, di Kirist. 
Colossians 2 3  Ci moom lañu denc lépp lu ñuy sàkku ci xel ak ci xam-xam. 
Colossians 2 4  Maa ngi wax lii, ngir kenn bañ leen a nax ci ay wax yu neex. 
Colossians 2 5  Jëmm ji ñëwul waaye sama xel a ngi ci yéen, di bég ci seen doxalin ak ngëm gu dëgër, gi ngeen am ci Kirist.    
Colossians 2 6  Kon nag, ni ngeen nangoo Kirist Yeesu ni Boroom bi, dundeleen noonu ci moom. 
Colossians 2 7  Saxleen ci moom, di màgg ci moom, tey gën a dëgër ci ngëm, gi ñu leen jàngal, ba seen xol di baawaan ci gërëm Yàlla.    
Colossians 2 8  Moytuleen ba kenn bañ leen a fàbbi ci ay xam-xami nit yuy naxi neen. Xam-xam yu mel noonu, ñu ngi soqikoo ci aada yu nit tëral, ci aaday àddina, waaye soqikoowul ci Kirist.    
Colossians 2 9  Ndaxte ci Kirist, maanaam ci yaramu nitam, la matug Yàlla gépp dëkk, 
Colossians 2 10  te mat ngeen ci moom, miy buuru kilifa yépp ak boroom sañ-sañ yépp. 
Colossians 2 11  Ndax seen ngëm ci moom xaraf ngeen xaraf bu loxol nit deful, maanaam Kirist summil na leen dooley bàkkaar, ji moomoon seen yaram. Loolu mooy xaraf, bi Kirist def. 
Colossians 2 12  Bi ñu leen sóobee ci ndox, suulaale nañu leen ak moom, te it dekki ngeen ak moom, ndaxte gëm ngeen ci dooley Yàlla, ji ko dekkal ca néew ya.    
Colossians 2 13  Te yéen ñi doon ndee fa kanam Yàlla ndax seeni moy ak seen ñàkka xaraf, Yàlla dundalaat na leen ak Kirist, baal nu sunuy bàkkaar yépp. 
Colossians 2 14  Mbind mi nu doon tiiñal, te daa nu yey ndax ay sàrtam, Yàlla far na ko, dindi ko, daajaale ko ca bant, ba Kirist deeye. 
Colossians 2 15  Futti na kilifa yi ak boroom sañ-sañ yi, weer leen ci kanamu ñépp, sëkktal leen niy jaam ndax ndam la Kirist jële ca bant ba.    
Colossians 2 16  Kon nag bu leen kenn teg tooñ ci li jëm ciy ñam mbaa naan, ci màggal mbaa xewu weer wu feeñ, mbaa ci bésu noflaay. 
Colossians 2 17  Loolu lépp nag takkandeer la woon buy misaal li waroon a ñëw, waaye lu dëggu li mi ngi ci Kirist. 
Colossians 2 18  Kuy bég ci di toroxlu ci ngistal, di jaamu ay malaaka, buleen ko may, mu àtte leen. Kooku dafay jeneer, di seet li koy feeñu, bay tiitaroo xalaatam, fekk xalaatu nit kese la, te neen. 
Colossians 2 19  Taqul ci Kirist, miy bopp bi yilif jëmm ji. Bopp bee tax ba jëmm jépp, ji siddit yi ak tenqo yi téye te taqale ko, di màgg màgg gi ko Yàlla di jox.    
Colossians 2 20  Ndegam deeyandoo ngeen ak Kirist, ba génne noonu ci aaday àddina, lu tax ngeen di nangu, ñu di leen teg ay sàrt yu mel nii: «Bul fab, bul ñam, bul laal,» ni bu seenug dund aju woon ci àddina si? 
Colossians 2 21  Sàrt yooyu ñu ngi aju ci ndigali nit ñi ak seen njàngale. Yëf yi ñu tudd yépp, dees na leen jariñoo, ba ñu jeex. 
Colossians 2 22  Dëgg la, seeni sàrt dañuy dénkaane pasteef ci jaamu Yàlla, di toroxlu ak di fitnaal seen yaram. Waaye sàrt yooyu nag amuñu benn njariñ, ngir nit ñi noot seen nafsu.
Colossians 3 1  Kon nag ndegam dekkeendoo ngeen ak Kirist, wutleen yëf, ya nekk ca kaw, fa Kirist toog ca ndeyjooru Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 2  Fonkleen yëf ya ca kaw, te ngeen bañ a faale yi ci suuf,
Colossians 3 3  ndaxte dee ngeen, te seen dund boole nañu ko ak Kirist, denc ca Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 4  Te bés bu Kirist miy seen dund feeñee, yéen itam dingeen feeñ ak moom ci biir ndam.    
Colossians 3 5  Kon nag li nekk ci yéen te bokk ci mbiri àddina, jébbal-leen ko dee, yu deme ni ndoxaanu yàqute, sobe, xemmem, bëgg-bëgg yu bon, ak bëgge, maanaam bokkaale Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 6  Yooyooy xëcc merum Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 7  Yéen itam noonu ngeen daan doxale bu jëkk, ba ngeen daan dunde noonu. 
Colossians 3 8  Waaye léegi bàyyileen yii yépp: mer, xadar, kiñaan ak di génne ci seen gémmiñ sos ak wax ju ñaaw. 
Colossians 3 9  Bàyyileen di fen seeni moroom, ndaxte summi ngeen jikko ju bon, ji ngeen judduwaale, moom ak ay jëfam; 
Colossians 3 10  te sol ngeen dund gu bees, gi Yàlla sàkk te di ko yeesal ba mu mel ni moom, ngir ngeen man koo xam bu wér. 
Colossians 3 11  Ci dund gu bees googu, amul Yawut ak ku dul Yawut, ku xaraf walla ku xaraful, jaam walla gor, ku jàngul ni Baarbaar yi, ak ku yeewuwul ni waa Sit, waaye Kirist ay lépp te dëkk ci ñépp.    
Colossians 3 12  Kon nag ndegam Yàlla tànn na leen, sellal leen, sopp leen, solooleen boog yërmande, laabiir, woyof, lewet ak muñ. 
Colossians 3 13  Muñalanteleen, di baalante, su amee kuy tawat moroomam. Baalanteleen, ni leen Boroom bi baale. 
Colossians 3 14  Ci kaw loolu lépp amleen mbëggeel, giy jókkaale lépp, ba mu mat.    
Colossians 3 15  Na jàmm ji Kirist di joxe noot seeni xol, ndaxte Yàlla woo na leen ci loolu, mel ni ay cér yu bokk benn yaram; te gërëmleen Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 16  Na kàddug Kirist dëkk ci yéen, bay baawaan, ngeen di jàngalante ak a artoonte ci seen biir ak xel mu mat sëkk, di woy ak a gërëm Yàlla ak seen xol bépp, ay taalifi Sabóor, ay kañ Yàlla ak ay cant yu tukkee ci Xelum Yàlla. 
Colossians 3 17  Te lu ngeen man a def, muy ci wax mbaa ci jëf, wéerleen ko ci turu Boroom bi Yeesu, jaare ci moom gërëm Yàlla Baay bi.    
Colossians 3 18  Jigéen ñi, na ku nekk nangul jëkkëram, ndaxte looloo jekk ci ñi bokk ci Boroom bi.    
Colossians 3 19  Góor ñi, na ku nekk bëgg jabaram te muñal ko.    
Colossians 3 20  Xale yi, déggal-leen seeni waajur ci lépp, ndaxte looloo rafet ci ñi bokk ci Boroom bi.    
Colossians 3 21  Baay yi, buleen bundaxataal seeni doom, ngir bañ a jeexal seen xol.    
Colossians 3 22  Jaam yi, nangul-leen ci lépp seen sang, yi ci àddina. Buleen ko def rekk ci seen kanam, di sàkku ngërëm, waaye na nekk lu dëggu ci yéen, ndax seen ragal Boroom bi. 
Colossians 3 23  Lu ngeen man a def, na ci seen xol tàlli; ngeen def ko ngir Boroom bi, te du ngir nit, 
Colossians 3 24  xam ne Boroom bi dina fey seeni jëf, mu di cér bi mu leen dencal. Kirist mooy Boroom, bi ngeen di liggéeyal. 
Colossians 3 25  Waaye ku def lu bon, Boroom bi dina la delloo sa jëf, te du gënale.
Colossians 4 1  Sang yi, yorleen seeni jaam ci nu jub te aw yoon, xam ne, am ngeen yéen itam ab Sang ca asamaan.    
Colossians 4 2  Dëkkleen ci ñaan Yàlla, farlu ci, boole ci ngërëm. 
Colossians 4 3  Te ngeen fasaale nu ci ñaan yi itam, ngir Yàlla ubbil nu bunt, nu man a xamle kàddoom, di yégle kumpa gi di Kirist, muy kumpa gi waral ñu jéng ma. 
Colossians 4 4  Ñaanleen ngir ma xamle ko ni mu ware.    
Colossians 4 5  Jëfeleen ak xel ci seen diggante ak waa àddina, te fu ngeen ame jot, fexeleen ba jariñoo ko. 
Colossians 4 6  Na seen wax jépp fees ak yiw te am xorom, ngir ngeen xam nan ngeen war a tontoo ku nekk.    
Colossians 4 7  Tisig, sama mbokk mi ma sopp, di jawriñ ju takku ak sama nawle ci liggéeyu Boroom bi, dina leen yégal lépp lu jëm ci samay mbir. 
Colossians 4 8  Lii moo tax ma yebal ko ci yéen: ngeen xam xebaar bi jóge ci nun, te it mu dëfël seen xol. 
Colossians 4 9  Onesim lay àndal, sunu mbokk mu takku, mi nu sopp, te mu bokk ci yéen. Dinañu leen xamal lépp lu xew fii.    
Colossians 4 10  Aristàrk mi nekk ak man ci kaso bi, mu ngi leen di nuyu, moom ak Màrk rakku Barnabas. Jot ngeen ay ndigal ci mbirum Màrk: bu ñëwee ci yéen, teral-leen ko. 
Colossians 4 11  Yeesu mi ñuy dàkkentale Yustus, moom it mu ngi leen di nuyu. Ñoom rekk ñooy Yawut yiy liggéeyandook man ngir nguuru Yàlla, te ñoo féexal sama xol. 
Colossians 4 12  Jaamu Kirist, Epafras, mi bokk ci yéen, mu ngi leen di nuyu. Du jóg ci di leen ñaanal, farlu ci ni kuy bëre, ngir ngeen taxaw temm ci coobareg Yàlla gépp, ànd ak ngëm gu mat ak kóolute gu wóor. 
Colossians 4 13  Maa ngi koy seedeel ne, mu ngi sonn bu baax ngir yéen, ngir waa Lawdise ak waa Yerapolis. 
Colossians 4 14  Luug, doktoor bi ñu sopp, mu ngi leen di nuyu, moom ak Demas. 
Colossians 4 15  Nuyul-leen nu mbokk, yi nekk Lawdise. Nuyul-leen nu itam Nimfa ak mbooloom ñi gëm, miy daje ci këram.    
Colossians 4 16  Bu ñu jàngee bataaxal bii ci yéen, fexeleen ba ñu jàng ko it ci mbooloom ñi gëm mi nekk Lawdise, te yéen it ngeen jàng bi ma yónnee waa Lawdise.    
Colossians 4 17  Te neleen Arkib: «Farlul ci sas, wi la Boroom bi sédde, ba matal ko.»    
Colossians 4 18  Man Pool maa leen di bind nuyoo bii ci sama loxob bopp. Fàttalikuleen ne, dañu maa jéng. Na yiwu Boroom bi ànd ak yéen!
1 Thessalonians 1 1  Nun Pool, Silwan ak Timote noo ngi leen di bind, yéen mbooloom ñi gëm ci dëkku Tesalonig te nekk ci Yàlla Baay bi ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist. Na yiw ak jàmm ànd ak yéen.    
1 Thessalonians 1 2  Bët bu set nu ngi sant Yàlla ndax yéen, di leen boole ci sunuy ñaan. 
1 Thessalonians 1 3  Dunu noppee fàttaliku ci kanam Yàlla sunu Baay jëf ji juddu ci seen ngëm, liggéey bi tukkee ci seen mbëggeel, ak muñ gi sosoo ci seen yaakaar ci sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist.    
1 Thessalonians 1 4  Bokk yi, yéen ñi Yàlla bëgg, xam nanu ne Yàlla tànn na leen;
1 Thessalonians 1 5  ndaxte xebaar bu baax, bi nu leen doon yégal, yemul woon ci ay wax rekk, waaye àndoon na ak kàttan ak Xel mu Sell mi ak kóolute gu mag. Xam ngeen sunu taxawaay ci seen biir ngir seen njariñ. 
1 Thessalonians 1 6  Te aw ngeen sunuy tànk ak yu Boroom bi, ci li ngeen nangu xebaar bi ci biir fitna yu metti, ànd ak mbég ci dooley Xel mu Sell mi. 
1 Thessalonians 1 7  Noonu ngeen daldi nekk royukaay ngir ñi gëm ñépp ci diiwaani Maseduwan ak Akayi. 
1 Thessalonians 1 8  Ndaxte kàddug Boroom bi jollee na ci seen biir, te yemul ci Maseduwan ak Akayi rekk, waaye seen gëm Yàlla siiw na fépp. Matul sax nu di ci wax dara,
1 Thessalonians 1 9  ndaxte ñoom ci seen bopp ñooy seede li sunu ngan def ci seen biir. Maanaam, ni ngeen dëddoo xërëm yi, jublu ci Yàlla te di ko jaamu, moom miy Yàlla Aji Dund ju dëggu ji, 
1 Thessalonians 1 10  te ngeen di séentu Doomam bàyyikoo asamaan, moom Yeesu mi mu dekkal te di nu musal ci merum Yàlla, mi nar a ñëw.
1 Thessalonians 2 1  Waaw bokk yi, xam ngeen ne, ngan gi nu leen ganesi woon du nganug neen. 
1 Thessalonians 2 2  Laata nuy ñëw, jaar nanu ci fitna ak toroxte ca dëkku Filib, ni ngeen ko xame; waaye Yàlla sunu Boroom may na nu fit, ba li tongoonte bi metti lépp it, yégal nanu leen xebaaru Yàlla bu baax bi. 
1 Thessalonians 2 3  Ndaxte sunu waaraate wéeruwul cig réer walla ci njublaŋ walla ciy nax. 
1 Thessalonians 2 4  Waaye gannaaw Yàlla moo nu seet, ba wóolu nu te dénk nu xebaar bu baax bi, kon noonu lanuy waaree, du ngir neex nit ñi, waaye ngir neex Yàlla, miy seet xol yi.    
1 Thessalonians 2 5  Musunoo jey kenn, yéen xam ngeen ko; sunu waare musul a ëmb bëgge, Yàlla seede na ko;
1 Thessalonians 2 6  musunoo sàkku ngërëmu nit, muy ci yéen, muy ci ñeneen. 
1 Thessalonians 2 7  Manoon nanoo diis ci seen kaw sax, nun ñiy ndawi Kirist, waaye woyofoon nanu ci seen biir, te lewet ni jaboot buy uuf doomam. 
1 Thessalonians 2 8  Cofeel gi nu am ci yéen tax na, bëggunu woon a yem ci xamal leen xebaaru Yàlla bu baax bi, waaye jox leen it sunu bakkan, ndaxte sunu xol seeyoon na ci yéen. 
1 Thessalonians 2 9  Bokk yi, yéena ngi fàttaliku sunu coono ak sunu ñaq; xam ngeen ni nu liggéeye guddi ak bëccëg, ngir bañ a diis ci seen kaw, ci di leen yégal xebaaru Yàlla.    
1 Thessalonians 2 10  Naka sunu diggante ak yéen ñi gëm, doxal nanu ko doxalin wu sell te jub te amul sikk: seede ngeen ko, te Yàlla it seede na ko. 
1 Thessalonians 2 11  Xam ngeen ne, dénk nanu leen kenn-kenn, ni baay di def ak doomam, dëfëlal leen seen xol te dëggal ci yéen, ngeen dund dund gu neex Yàlla, moom mi leen di woo, ngeen séddu ci nguuram ak ndamam.    
1 Thessalonians 2 12  Te it dunu noppee sant Yàlla ci lii: ba ngeen jotee kàddug Yàlla, gi nu doon waare, nangu ngeen ko, waxuma ni kàddug nit waaye ni kàddug Yàlla, ndaxte moom la ci dëgg-dëgg, te mu ngi jëf ci yéen ñi gëm. 
1 Thessalonians 2 13  Ndaxte bokk yi, aw ngeen ci tànki mboolooy Yàlla, yi nekk ca réewu Yawut ya tey daje ci turu Kirist Yeesu; fitna ya ñu daj ca Yawut ya, yéen it seen waa réew teg nañu leen ko. 
1 Thessalonians 2 14  Ñoom Yawut yi rey nañu Boroom bi Yeesu, ni ñu reye woon yonent yi; teg nañu nu fitna yu metti; neexuñu Yàlla, ànduñu ak kenn, 
1 Thessalonians 2 15  di nu teree wax ak ñi dul Yawut, ngir bañ ñu mucc. Duñu noppee xuus ci biir bàkkaar, waaye merum Yàlla xëppu na ci seen kaw.    
1 Thessalonians 2 16  Nun nag bokk yi, ba ñu ma leen xañee ab diir --xol yi taxul may wax, waaye jëmm yi rekk — jéem nanu leen a gis ak sunu kem-kàttan, ndax namm nanu leen, ba sunu xol seey ci gis leen. 
1 Thessalonians 2 17  Kon jàppoon nanu leen a seetsi — man Pool sax ay yooni yoon, waaye Seytaane téq na ma. 
1 Thessalonians 2 18  Ndaxte bés bu Yeesu sunu Boroom dellusee, te nu fekke ko, kan mooy sunu yaakaar? Kan mooy sunu mbég? Kan mooy sunu kaala, gi nuy tiitaroo? 
1 Thessalonians 2 19  Xanaa du yéen? Waaw yéenay sunu ndam, yéenay sunu mbég.
1 Thessalonians 3 1  Kon nag, ba nu ko mënatul a dékku, nangu nanu ñu bàyyi nu, nun doŋŋ, ca dëkku Aten,
1 Thessalonians 3 2  te yónni nanu Timote, sunu mbokk ak sunu nawle ci liggéeyu Yàlla ak ci waareb xebaaru Kirist. Yónni nanu ko, ngir mu dénk leen, tey feddali seen ngëm,
1 Thessalonians 3 3  ngir kenn bañ a raf ndax nattu, yi ngeen di jaar. Yéen ci seen bopp xam ngeen ne, nattu mooy sunu cér. 
1 Thessalonians 3 4  Ba nu nekkee ak yéen sax, waxoon nanu leen, waxati ko ne, fàww nu sonn; te noonu la ame, yéen xam ngeen ko. 
1 Thessalonians 3 5  Noonu ba ma ko mënatul a dékku, yónnee naa, ngir xam fu seen ngëm tollu, ngir ragal Seytaane fiir leen, ba sunu ñaq neen.    
1 Thessalonians 3 6  Waaye léegi Timote bawoo na ci yéen, indaale xebaar yu neex ci seen ngëm ak seen mbëggeel; xamal na nu ne, yéena ngi am pàttaliku yu rafet ci nun te namm nu lool, ni nu leen namme yéen itam. 
1 Thessalonians 3 7  Noonu bokk yi, ci biir tiis ak coono yi nu nekk, seen ngëm dëfël na sunu xol. 
1 Thessalonians 3 8  Ndaxte noo ngi dund dëgg-dëgg, ndegam yéena ngi sax ci Boroom bi. 
1 Thessalonians 3 9  Ndaw cant yu bare yu nu war a sant Yàlla ndax yéen! Ndaw mbég mu bare, mi nu am ci kanamam ndax yéen! 
1 Thessalonians 3 10  Guddi ak bëccëg nu ngi wàkkirlu ci ñaan Yàlla, ngir gis leen, ba man a mottali seen ngëm.    
1 Thessalonians 3 11  Na Yàlla sunu Baay moom ci boppam ak Yeesu sunu Boroom jubal sunu yoon ci yéen. 
1 Thessalonians 3 12  Na leen Boroom bi dolli mbëggeel gu tar, ngeen bëggante te bëgg ñépp, ni nu leen bëgge nun. 
1 Thessalonians 3 13  Na samp seeni xol noonu ci cell gu amul sikk fa kanam Yàlla sunu Baay, ba bés bu Yeesu sunu Boroom dellusee, ànd ak gaayam yu sell yépp.
1 Thessalonians 4 1  Léegi nag bokk yi, jot ngeen ci nun, nan ngeen war a dunde ba neex Yàlla, te moom ngeen di def. Waaye ci turu Boroom bi Yeesu nu ngi leen di ñaan ak a dénk, ngeen gën koo feddali. 
1 Thessalonians 4 2  Ndaxte xam ngeen ndigal, yi nu leen jox ci wàllu Yeesu Boroom bi. 
1 Thessalonians 4 3  Lii nag mooy coobareg Yàlla: ngeen sell, maanaam ngeen moytu njaaloo;
1 Thessalonians 4 4  ngeen noot seeni cér ci cell ak tedd,
1 Thessalonians 4 5  te xemmem bañ leen a jiital, ni xeeti àddina yi xamul Yàlla. 
1 Thessalonians 4 6  Ci mbir mii nag, bu kenn ci yéen laal yëfi jaambur, ngir bañ koo tooñ. Ndaxte waxoon nanu leen bu yàgg te artu leen ne, ñiy def loolu, Boroom bi dina leen mbugal. 
1 Thessalonians 4 7  Ndaxte Yàlla woo na nu, nu dund ci cell, waaye du ci sobe. 
1 Thessalonians 4 8  Ku tanqamlu wax jii nag, defoo ko nit, Yàlla nga ko def, moom mi leen di jox Xel mu Sell mi.    
1 Thessalonians 4 9  Ci lu jëm ci bëggante ci seen biir, matul nu leen di bind dara, ndaxte Yàlla def na ci seen xol, ngeen bëggante. 
1 Thessalonians 4 10  Te moom ngeen di def ci bokk yépp, yi ci diiwaanu Maseduwan. Waaye bokk yi, maa ngi leen di xiirtal, ngeen gën cee sax. 
1 Thessalonians 4 11  Fullawooleen a dund ci jàmm, di topptoo seen mbiri bopp tey lekk seen ñaq, ni nu leen ko sante woon. 
1 Thessalonians 4 12  Noonu dingeen dund dund gu jekk ci kanamu waa àddina, te it dungeen soxlaal kenn dara.    
1 Thessalonians 4 13  Ci mbirum ñi nelaw nag bokk yi, bëgguñu ngeen réere mbir, ba tiis ni aji gëmul, yi amul benn yaakaar. 
1 Thessalonians 4 14  Ndegam gëm nanu ne, Yeesu dee na te dekki, noonu it Yàlla dina indaale ak Yeesu ñépp ñi ko gëm te nelaw.    
1 Thessalonians 4 15  Nu ngi leen di wax lii tukkee ci Boroom bi: nun ñiy dund te des fi, ba kera Boroom biy dellusi, dunu jiitu ñi nelaw. 
1 Thessalonians 4 16  Ndaxte ndigal lu jamp dina jib, baatu kilifa ci malaaka yi dégtu, liitu Yàlla jolli, te Boroom bi moom ci boppam dina wàcce ca asamaan. Booba ñi gëm Kirist te dee dinañu jëkk a dekki; 
1 Thessalonians 4 17  gannaaw loolu nun ñiy dund te des fi, dinañu ne fëyy ak ñoom jëm ci niir yi, taseji ak Boroom bi ci jaww ji. Te noonu dinanu nekk ak Boroom bi ba fàww. 
1 Thessalonians 4 18  Kon nag na ku nekk di dëfël sa xolu moroom ak kàddu yooyu.
1 Thessalonians 5 1  Waaye bokk yi, ci li jëm ci jamono yi ak waxtu, yi loolu di am, matul nu leen ciy bind dara. 
1 Thessalonians 5 2  Ndaxte xam ngeen bu wér ne, ni sàcc di ñëwe guddi, noonu la bésu Boroom bi di ñëwe. 
1 Thessalonians 5 3  Fekk nit ñiy naan: «Lépp a ngi ci jàmm, ba ne leww,» booba musiba bett leen, ni aw mat di bette jigéen ju ëmb, te kenn du ci mucc. 
1 Thessalonians 5 4  Waaye yéen bokk yi, nekkuleen cig lëndëm, ba tax bés boobu bett leen ni sàcc. 
1 Thessalonians 5 5  Ndaxte yéen ñépp ci leer ak bëccëg ngeen bokk; bokkunu ci guddi ak lëndëm. 
1 Thessalonians 5 6  Kon nag bunu nelaw ni ñeneen ñi, waaye nanu xool te maandu. 
1 Thessalonians 5 7  Ndaxte ñiy nelaw, guddi lañuy nelaw, te ñiy màndi, guddi lañuy màndi. 
1 Thessalonians 5 8  Waaye nun ñiy waa bëccëg, nanu maandu te ràngoo ngir xare bi: ngëm ak mbëggeel, muy kiiraayu dënn, ak kóoluteg mucc, muy mbaxanam xare. 
1 Thessalonians 5 9  Ndaxte Yàlla jaglewu nu meram, waaye mucc la nu jagleel ndax darajay sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist. 
1 Thessalonians 5 10  Deeyal na nu, ngir nu man a dund ak moom, bu nu nelawee ak bu nu nelawagul. 
1 Thessalonians 5 11  Kon nag nangeen dëgëralante te yokkante seen ngëm, ni ngeen koy defe.    
1 Thessalonians 5 12  Gannaaw loolu bokk yi, ci lu jëm ci njiit, yi Boroom bi teg ci seen kanam te ñuy liggéey ci seen biir, di leen artu, maa ngi leen di ñaan ngeen déglu leen; 
1 Thessalonians 5 13  rax-ca-dolli ngeen naw leen seen kem-kàttan te bëgg leen ndax seen liggéey. Na jàmm am ci seen biir. 
1 Thessalonians 5 14  Bokk yi, nu ngi leen di dénk, ngeen yedd ñi feñaag, dëfël ñi seen yasara yàcciku, dimbali ñi néew doole, tey muñal ñépp. 
1 Thessalonians 5 15  Saxleen ci baax ci seen biir ak ci ñépp, te bañ a feyantoo. 
1 Thessalonians 5 16  Deeleen bég 
1 Thessalonians 5 17  te sax ciy ñaan Yàlla, 
1 Thessalonians 5 18  di ko gërëm ci lépp, ndaxte loolu mooy coobareg Yàlla ci yéen ci seen bokk ci Kirist Yeesu. 
1 Thessalonians 5 19  Buleen fey taalu Xelum Yàlla, 
1 Thessalonians 5 20  di xeeb waxu yonent yi. 
1 Thessalonians 5 21  Waaye seetleen mbir yépp, jàpp ci li baax, 
1 Thessalonians 5 22  dëddu lépp lu ci bon.    
1 Thessalonians 5 23  Na leen Yàlla Boroom jàmm sellal, ba ngeen mat sëkk; na sàmm seen xel mépp, seen xol bépp ak seen yaram wépp, ngir dara bañ cee am sikk, ba bés bu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist dellusee. 
1 Thessalonians 5 24  Yàlla, mi leen woo ci loolu, kuy sàmm kóllëre la, te dina ko def.    
1 Thessalonians 5 25  Bokk yi, buleen nu fàtte ci seeni ñaan.    
1 Thessalonians 5 26  Nuyul-leen nu bokk yépp ak saafoonte bu laab. 
1 Thessalonians 5 27  Maa ngi leen di dénk ci kanamu Boroom bi, ngeen jàngal bataaxal bii bokk yépp.    
1 Thessalonians 5 28  Na yiwu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist ànd ak yéen.
2 Thessalonians 1 1  Nun Pool ak Silwan ak Timote noo leen di bind, yéen mbooloom ñi gëm ci dëkku Tesalonig te nekk ci Yàlla sunu Baay ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist. 
2 Thessalonians 1 2  Na leen Yàlla Baay bi ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist may yiw ak jàmm.    
2 Thessalonians 1 3  Bokk yi, mënunu lu dul sax ci sant Yàlla ndax yéen. Loolu jaadu na, ndax seen ngëm di gën a sax, te mbëggeel gi ngeen am ci seen biir, ku nekk ci sa moroom, di yokku lu bare. 
2 Thessalonians 1 4  Noonu nu ngi damu ci yéen ci kanamu mboolooy Yàlla yi, ndax seen muñ ak seen ngëm ci biir mboolem fitnay noon, ak coono, yi ngeen di dékku.    
2 Thessalonians 1 5  Loolu mooy firndeel àtteb Yàlla bu jub bi, di wone ne yelloo ngeen nguuru Yàlla, gi tax ngeen di sonn. 
2 Thessalonians 1 6  Ndaxte jub na ci Yàlla, mu delloo coono ñi leen di sonal,
2 Thessalonians 1 7  te it yéen ñiy dékku coono, mu boole leen ak nun, tàbbal nu ci noflaay, bés bu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist jógee asamaan, feeñ fi. Keroog dina ànd ak malaakaam yu am kàttan,
2 Thessalonians 1 8  safara su yànj wër ko, mu feeñ ngir mbugal ñi xamul Yàlla te bañ a déggal xebaar bu baaxu sunu Boroom Yeesu. 
2 Thessalonians 1 9  Seen pey mooy alku ba fàww, ñu dàq leen fu sore Boroom bi ak ndamam lu réy. 
2 Thessalonians 1 10  Dina ñëw bés booba, ngir ndamam jolli ci biir gaayam yu sell yi, te ñépp ñi ko gëm yéemu ci moom — te ci ngeen bokk, ndaxte gëm ngeen li nu leen seede.    
2 Thessalonians 1 11  Moo tax dunu noppeek di leen ñaanal, ngir Yàlla sunu Boroom def leen, ngeen yeyoo li tax mu woo leen, te yeggali ak doole ci yéen bépp yéene ju baax ak bépp jëfu ngëm. 
2 Thessalonians 1 12  Noonu turu Yeesu sunu Boroom dina màgg ci yéen, te yéen it dingeen màgg ci moom, aju ci yiwu sunu Yàlla ak Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist.
2 Thessalonians 2 1  Ci lu jëm ci ñëwu Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist nag, bokk yi, ak sunu daje ak moom, am na lu ma leen di ñaan:
2 Thessalonians 2 2  bu leen kenn gaaw a tàggale ak seen sago, mbaa di leen jaaxal, muy yonent buy wax, muy kàddu mbaa bataaxal bu ñu nu moomaleel, ci ne leen bésu Boroom bi ñëw na xaat. 
2 Thessalonians 2 3  Bu leen kenn nax ci benn fànn, ndaxte balaa booba, fàww Xiiroo bu mag bi ak Yàlla am, te Nitu ñaawteef ki feeñ, moom aji alku ji. 
2 Thessalonians 2 4  Day weddi lépp lu ñu teg Yàlla walla ñu koy jaamu, di yékkati boppam, ba toog sax ca kër Yàlla ga, tudde boppam Yàlla.    
2 Thessalonians 2 5  Xanaa fàttalikuwuleen ne, waxoon naa leen ko, ba ma nekkee ak yéen. 
2 Thessalonians 2 6  Te xam ngeen li ko téye léegi, ba du man a feeñ lu dul ci waxtoom. 
2 Thessalonians 2 7  Ndaxte fi mu ne ñaawteef gaa ngi jax-jaxi xaat ci kumpa, waaye ki ko téye mi ngi fi ba tey. Bu fi jógee nag,
2 Thessalonians 2 8  Nitu ñaawteef ki dina feeñ, te Boroom bi Yeesu dina ko rey ak ngelawul gémmiñam, tas ko ak leer giy ànd ak ñëwam. 
2 Thessalonians 2 9  Bu Nitu ñaawteef kooku feeñee, dina ànd ak kàttanu Seytaane ak doole ju bare, di wone ay firnde ak ay kéemaan yu dul dëgg; 
2 Thessalonians 2 10  te dina nas bépp naxe buy sànke, ba yéem ñi nar a alku, ndaxte ubbiluñu seeni xol dëgg, gi leen manoon a musal. 
2 Thessalonians 2 11  Looloo tax Yàlla yónnee leen xelum réer, ba ñu gëm fen. 
2 Thessalonians 2 12  Noonu Yàlla dina mbugal ñépp ñi gëmul woon dëgg te doon bànneexu ci njubadi.    
2 Thessalonians 2 13  Kon nag bokk yi, yéen ñi Boroom bi bëgg, mënunu lu dul sax ci sant Yàlla ci li mu leen tànn ca njàlbéen ga, ngir musal leen, mu sédde leen boppam jaarale ko ci jëfu Xel mu Sell mi ak seen gëm dëgg gi. 
2 Thessalonians 2 14  Te Yàlla woo na leen ci loolu jaarale ko ci xebaar bu baax, bi nu leen doon yégal, ngir ngeen bokk ci ndamu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist. 
2 Thessalonians 2 15  Kon nag bokk yi, taxawleen bu dëgër te jàpp ci dénkaane yi nu leen jottali, muy ci li nu wax, muy ci li nu bind.    
2 Thessalonians 2 16  Na sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist moom ci boppam ak Yàlla sunu Baay, mi nu bëgg te wone yiwam ci nun, ba ubbil nu buntu jàmm ju sax ak yaakaar ju wér, 
2 Thessalonians 2 17  dëfël seeni xol te saxal leen ci bépp jëf ju rafet ak gépp kàddu gu baax.
2 Thessalonians 3 1  Léegi nag bokk yi, ñaanal-leen nu, ngir kàddug Boroom bi law te ànd ak ndam, ni mu ko ame woon ci yéen. 
2 Thessalonians 3 2  Ngeen ñaanal nu it, ngir nu mucc ci ñi bon te soxor, ndaxte du ñépp a gëm. 
2 Thessalonians 3 3  Waaye Boroom bi kuy sàmm kóllëre la; dina leen dëgëral te musal leen ci Ibliis. 
2 Thessalonians 3 4  Te wóor nanu ci kanamu Boroom bi ne, yéena ngi def li nu leen santoon, te dingeen ci sax. 
2 Thessalonians 3 5  Na Boroom bi gindi seeni xol ci mbëggeelu Yàlla ak muñu Kirist.    
2 Thessalonians 3 6  Nu ngi leen di sant it bokk yi, ci turu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist, ngeen dëddu bépp mbokk buy wéy ci tayel te bañ a topp dénkaane, yi nu leen jottali. 
2 Thessalonians 3 7  Xam ngeen bu baax, yéen ci seen bopp, ni ngeen war a awe ci sunuy tànk. Ba nu nekkee ca yéen, wéyunu woon ci tayel
2 Thessalonians 3 8  te musunoo lekk ñaqu kenn. Waaye guddi ak bëccëg danu daan ñaq, di sonn, ngir bañ a wéeru ci kenn ci yéen. 
2 Thessalonians 3 9  Waxuma ne amunu sañ-sañu def ko, waaye danoo bëggoon a nekk ay royukaay ci yéen, ngir ngeen aw ci sunuy tànk. 
2 Thessalonians 3 10  Ndaxte ba nu nekkee ca yéen, lii lanu tëraloon: «Ku liggéeyul, du lekk.»    
2 Thessalonians 3 11  Léegi nag dégg nanu ne, am na ci yéen ñuy wéy ci tayel; liggéeyuñu dara, lu dul di dugg ci lu seen yoon nekkul. 
2 Thessalonians 3 12  Ñu deme noonu nag, nu ngi leen di sant te di leen dénk ci turu Boroom bi Yeesu Kirist, ñuy liggéey ci jàmm tey dunde seen ñaq. 
2 Thessalonians 3 13  Yéen nag bokk yi, buleen tàyyi ci def lu rafet.    
2 Thessalonians 3 14  Su kenn bañee topp li nu bind ci bataaxal bii, ràññeeleen ko te sore ko, ngir mu rus ci. 
2 Thessalonians 3 15  Waxuma ngeen def ko noon, waaye ngeen yedd ko ni seen mbokk.    
2 Thessalonians 3 16  Na leen Boroom jàmm may jàmm ci fépp ak ci lépp. Na Boroom bi ànd ak yéen ñépp.    
2 Thessalonians 3 17  Tàggoo bii maa ko bind ci sama loxo, man Pool. Nii laay binde, te di màndargaale nii sama bataaxal yépp. 
2 Thessalonians 3 18  Na yiwu sunu Boroom Yeesu Kirist ànd ak yéen ñépp.
1 Timothy 1 1  Man Pool, ndawul Kirist Yeesu ci ndigalu Yàlla sunu Musalkat ak Kirist Yeesu sunu yaakaar,
1 Timothy 1 2  maa ngi lay bind Timote, yaw miy sama doomu diine ju wér. Na la Yàlla Baay bi ak Kirist Yeesu sunu Boroom may yiw, yërmande ak jàmm.    
1 Timothy 1 3  Xam nga ne, ba may dem diiwaanu Maseduwan, ñaanoon naa la, nga des dëkku Efes, ngir dénk ña fa doon jàngale luy sànke, ñu bàyyi ko. 
1 Timothy 1 4  Te it nga dénk leen, ñu bañ a topp léebi diiney neen ak limi maam yu dul jeex mukk. Loolu werante rekk lay jur, waaye du jëme kanam mbir mi Yàlla tëral, wéer ko ci ngëm. 
1 Timothy 1 5  Waaye li sunuy dénkaane di jur mooy mbëggeel gu jóge ci xol bu laab, ci xel mu dal ak ci ngëm gu wér. 
1 Timothy 1 6  Am na ñu moy loolu, ba jeng jëm ciy waxi neen. 
1 Timothy 1 7  Dañoo sababloo nekk ay jàngalekat ci yoonu Musaa, fekk xamuñu dara sax ci li ñuy wax ak a dëggal.    
1 Timothy 1 8  Ci li aju ci yoonu Musaa nag, xam nanu ne baax na, ci ku koy jëfe ni ko Yàlla tërale. 
1 Timothy 1 9  Xam nanu it ne, tëddul ngir ñi jub waaye ngir ñi jubadi ak ñi déggadi, ñi weddi tey bàkkaar, ñi selladi te fonkadi Yàlla, ñiy dóor ndey walla baay, ak ñiy bóom; 
1 Timothy 1 10  ngir ñiy doxaan, ñi góor-jigéenu ak ñiy def nit jaam, ñiy fen tey wann seen kàddu, ak lépp luy juuyoo ak njàngale mu wér 
1 Timothy 1 11  mu xebaar bu baax bi indaale. Te xamleb xebaar, boobuy feeñal ndamu Yàlla Aji Tedd ji, dénk nañu ma ko.    
1 Timothy 1 12  Maa ngi gërëm sunu Boroom Kirist Yeesu, mi ma dooleel, ci kóolute gi mu am ci man, ba fal ma jawriñ. 
1 Timothy 1 13  Moona daa naa suufeel turam, di fitnaal ak a toroxal ñi ko gëm. Waaye Yàlla yërëm na ma, ndaxte ñàkka xam ak ñàkka gëm rekk a taxoon ma def ko. 
1 Timothy 1 14  Te yiwu sunu Boroom baawaan na ci man, ànd ak ngëm ak mbëggeel, yi bawoo ci Kirist Yeesu. 
1 Timothy 1 15  Wax ju wóor a ngii te yelloo gépp kóolute: Kirist Yeesu ganesi na àddina, ngir musal bàkkaarkat yi, te maa ci raw! 
1 Timothy 1 16  Waaye Yàlla yërëm na ma, ngir Kirist Yeesu jëkk a feeñal ci man muñam gu yaatu gi, ma nekk royukaay ci ñi ko nar a gëm te am dund gu dul jeex. 
1 Timothy 1 17  Yaw Buur bi fiy sax ba abadan, yaw mi bët mënta gis, yaw Yàlla miy kenn, yaa yelloo teraanga ak ndam ba fàww. Amiin!    
1 Timothy 1 18  Kon nag Timote sama doom, loolu mooy sas wi ma lay dénk, te mu dëppook waxi yonent, yi jëmoon ci yaw. Doolewool wax yooyu, ba xeex xeex bu baax bi, 
1 Timothy 1 19  di sàmm sa ngëm ak xel mu dal. Am na ñu seen xel nëx, ba labal seen ngëm, 
1 Timothy 1 20  naka Imene ak Alegsàndar; jébbal naa leen Seytaane, ngir ñu réccu li ñu doon sosal Yàlla.
1 Timothy 2 1  Fii laay tàmbale nag: maa ngi leen di dénk, ngeen yóbbu ñépp fa kanam Yàlla ciy ñaan, ay tinu ak i ngërëm. 
1 Timothy 2 2  Ñaanal-leen buur yi ak kilifa yépp, ngir nu man a am dund gu dal te jàmmu, ànd ak ragal Yàlla ak faayda yu mat.    
1 Timothy 2 3  Loolu mooy li rafet te neex Yàlla sunu Musalkat,
1 Timothy 2 4  bi bëgg ñépp mucc te xam dëgg gi. 
1 Timothy 2 5  Ndaxte jenn Yàlla kepp moo am, ak benn Rammukat kepp diggante Yàlla ak nit ñi, di nit ki Kirist Yeesu,
1 Timothy 2 6  mi joxe bakkanam ngir jot ñépp. Loolu mooy seede si Yàlla joxe, bi waxtu wi jotee. 
1 Timothy 2 7  Te fal na ma ci ndaw ak jàngalekat, may yégal xeeti àddina yoonu ngëm ak dëgg; fenuma, dëgg rekk laay wax.    
1 Timothy 2 8  Li ma bëgg kon mooy lii: na góor ñi ñaan ci Yàlla fu nekk, tàllal ko loxo yu sell, te bañ cee boole mer mbaa werante. 
1 Timothy 2 9  Naka noonu itam, na jigéen ñi di sol col gu faaydawu, cig woyof ak maandu. Buñu def seen xel ciy létt ak ci takkaayu wurus, mbaa ciy per ak col gu jafe. 
1 Timothy 2 10  Waaye na seen col di jëf yu rafet, ndaxte looloo jekk ci jigéen juy woote ag ragal Yàlla.    
1 Timothy 2 11  Te it na jigéen jàng cig noppi, ànd ak déggal gu mat. 
1 Timothy 2 12  Mayuma jigéen, muy jàngale mbaa muy jiite góor, waaye na noppi. 
1 Timothy 2 13  Ndaxte Aadama la Yàlla jëkk a sàkk, door caa teg Awa. 
1 Timothy 2 14  Te it du Aadama la Seytaane nax, waaye jigéen ja la nax, ba mu jàdd. 
1 Timothy 2 15  Teewul jigéen dina mucc ci wasin, su saxee ci ngëm ak mbëggeel, di ku sell te maandu.
1 Timothy 3 1  Wax ju wóor a ngii: kuy sabablu yenub sàmm mbooloo mi, mu ngi yóotu liggéey bu rafet. 
1 Timothy 3 2  Sàmm bi nag, nii la war a mel: war na ñàkk ŋàññ, yem ci benn soxna, moom boppam te maandu; war na am faayda, man gan te am mayu jàngale;
1 Timothy 3 3  warul di ab màndikat mbaa xeexkat, waaye na lewet te jàmmu, bañ a bëgge ci xaalis. 
1 Timothy 3 4  Na yor këram yorin wu rafet, te ay doomam déggal ko ak teggin yu mat. 
1 Timothy 3 5  Ndaxte ku mënta yor njabootam, naka lay man a yore njabootu Yàlla?
1 Timothy 3 6  Te it bumu nekk kuy door a gëm, ngir mu bañ a yég boppam, bay dajeek mbugalu Yàlla, ni ko Seytaane defe woon. 
1 Timothy 3 7  Te it war na am seede su rafet ci waa àddina, ngir ñu bañ koo diiŋat, ba muy daanu ci fiiru Seytaane.    
1 Timothy 3 8  Kiy topptoo li mbooloo miy jëfandikoo itam na am faayda te fonk kàddoom; bumu di ku yàqu ci sangara, mbaa ku alal jiital. 
1 Timothy 3 9  Na sàmm mbóoti ngëm gi ak xel mu dal. 
1 Timothy 3 10  Moom itam nañu ko jëkk a seetlu, ba mu leer ne amul ŋàññ, ñu door koo fal. 
1 Timothy 3 11  Naka noonu, na jigéen ñi am faayda, bañ a jëw mbaa xér ci dara, waaye nañu takku ci lépp.    
1 Timothy 3 12  Ku ñu dénk sasu topptoo yëfi mbooloo mi nag, nay ku yem ci benn soxna, jiite bu baax këram ak i doomam. 
1 Timothy 3 13  Ndaxte ku ci rafetal sasam dina am tur wu tedd ak kóolute gu mat sëkk ci yoonu ngëm, gi ci Kirist Yeesu.    
1 Timothy 3 14  Bëgg naa laa seetsi balaa yàgg, 
1 Timothy 3 15  waaye amaana mu yéex. Moo tax ma lay bind bataaxal bii, ngir xamal la, ni ñu war a nekke ci kër Yàlla gi, maanaam ci mbooloom Yàlla Aji Dund ji, miy kenug dëgg te di sëslaayam. 
1 Timothy 3 16  Ci dëgg-dëgg ragal Yàlla ëmb na mbóot yu xóot:Ki wàcc, yor bindu nit,mu bir ne xelam jub na,te malaaka ya gis ko;xamlees na ko ci xeet yi,ñu gëm ko ci kaw suuf,te Yàlla teeru ko ci ndamam.
1 Timothy 4 1  Xelum Yàlla mi wax na bu leer ne, ci mujug jamono dina am ñu bàyyi yoonu ngëm wi, di topp ay xel yuy fàbbee ak xalaati Seytaane. 
1 Timothy 4 2  Ñooñu ay naaféq yuy naxe lañu, te seen xol dërkiis. 
1 Timothy 4 3  Dinañu tere séy, di araamal ay ñam, fekk Yàlla sàkk na leen, ngir ñi gëm te xam dëgg man ciy jëfandiku ak cant. 
1 Timothy 4 4  Ndaxte li Yàlla sàkk lépp baax na, kon wenn ñam araamul ci ku koy jëfandikoo ak cant. 
1 Timothy 4 5  Ndaxte kàddug Yàlla ak ñaan ñoo koy sellal.    
1 Timothy 4 6  Saxal ci digal bokk yi loolu nag, kon dinga nekk jawriñu Kirist Yeesu ju baax ju regg ci kàdduy yoonu ngëm wi ak njàngale mu rafet, mi nga xam bu wér. 
1 Timothy 4 7  Tanqamlul ay léebi diiney neen, di ay wax yu amul bopp yu àddina kese; waaye tàggatal sa bopp ci ragal Yàlla. 
1 Timothy 4 8  Ndaxte tàggat yaram am na fu njariñam yem, waaye njariñu ragal Yàlla dafa daj lépp, ëmb digey àddina ak àllaaxira. 
1 Timothy 4 9  Wax ju wóor a ngii, te mat a nangu ak gépp kóolute. 
1 Timothy 4 10  Danuy ñaq tey bëre, ndaxte wékk nanu sunu yaakaar ci Yàlla Aji Dund ji, di Musalkatu ñépp, rawatina nag ci ñi gëm.    
1 Timothy 4 11  Digal leen yëf yooyu nag ci sa njàngale. 
1 Timothy 4 12  Bu la kenn xeeb ndax say at, waaye defal sa bopp royukaayu ñi gëm ci say wax ak say jëf, ci sa mbëggeel, sa ngëm ak sa cell. 
1 Timothy 4 13  Li feek may dikk, saxal ci jàng di biral Mbind mi ci mbooloo mi, di leen dénk ak a jàngal. 
1 Timothy 4 14  Bul sàggane may gi nekk ci yaw, gi la Yàlla jox jaarale ko ci waxu yonent, keroog bi la njiit yi tegee loxo. 
1 Timothy 4 15  Faaydaalal yëf yooyu te sóobu ci, ba sa jëm kanam bir ñépp. 
1 Timothy 4 16  Sàmmal sa bopp te sàmm sa njàngale, te sax ci; noonu dinga musal sa bopp, yaw ak ñi lay déglu.
1 Timothy 5 1  Bul gëdd mag, waaye waxtaanal ak moom ni sa baay. Ndaw it, nga digal ko ni sa rakk,
1 Timothy 5 2  jigéen ju mag, def ko ni sa yaay; ju ndaw, ni sa jigéen ak cell gu mat sëkk.    
1 Timothy 5 3  Ci wàllu ñi seen jëkkër faatu nag, ku ci sësul ci kenn, teral ko ngir Yàlla. 
1 Timothy 5 4  Waaye ku ci am ay doom mbaa ay sët, na njaboot googu jëkk a wone seen ragal Yàlla ci seen biir kër, ci delloo njukkal seen waajur, ndaxte loolu lu rafet la fa kanam Yàlla.    
1 Timothy 5 5  Jigéen ju sësul ci kenn day wékk yaakaaram jépp ci Yàlla, sax ci di ko wéetal te di ko ñaan guddi ak bëccëg. 
1 Timothy 5 6  Waaye ki bànneex jiital, ndee luy dox la. 
1 Timothy 5 7  Dénk leen loolu, ngir ñu bañ a am benn gàkk. 
1 Timothy 5 8  Ndaxte ki defalul ay bokkam dara, rawatina ay waajuram, weddi na yoonu ngëm wi, ba yées ku gëmadi.    
1 Timothy 5 9  Ku bëgg a bindu ci ñi seen jëkkër faatu, nii la war a mel: war na wees juróom-benn-fukki at, di jigéen ju yemoon ci jëkkëram, 
1 Timothy 5 10  te mu ràññiku ci jëf yu rafet yu deme ni yar ay guneem, man gan, geestu gaayi Yàlla yu sell yi, dimbali ñi nekk ci tiis; maanaa di ku takku ci mboolem jëf yu rafet yi.    
1 Timothy 5 11  Waaye bul bind jigéen ju ndaw, ndaxte bu ko ay bëgg-bëggam xiiree ci sore Kirist, dina bëgg a séyaat, 
1 Timothy 5 12  te dina daje ak mbugal ndaxte fecci na kóllëre. 
1 Timothy 5 13  Te du yem ci bëgg a séyaat rekk, waaye ku tayel lay doon; di ku wër kër ak kër, rax-ca-dolli réy làmmiñ te deñ kumpa, di wax lu yoonam nekkul. 
1 Timothy 5 14  Looloo tax ma bëgg, jigéen yu ndaw yi séyaat, am ay doom, yor seeni kër, ba seen benn noon du leen man a gàkkal. 
1 Timothy 5 15  Ndaxte fi mu ne sax am na ñu jeng xaat, ba topp Seytaane.    
1 Timothy 5 16  Kon nag jigéen ju gëm te am mbokk mu jëkkëram faatu, na ko dimbali te bañ koo bàyyeek mbooloom ñi gëm. Noonu mbooloo mi dina man a dimbali jigéen ñi sësul ci kenn.    
1 Timothy 5 17  Li jëm ci njiiti mbooloo mi nag, joxal teraanga ju mat sëkk ñi ciy rafetal seen liggéey, rawatina ñi sax dàkk ci waare bi ak njàngale mi. 
1 Timothy 5 18  Ndaxte Mbind mi nee na: «Bul sunjuñ gémmiñu nag wu ñu takk bojjukaay,» nee na it: «Ku ñaq, jariñu.» 
1 Timothy 5 19  Kuy tuumaal njiit fi yaw, bu ko gëm, li feek ñaar walla ñetti seede dëggaluñu ko. 
1 Timothy 5 20  Waaye ñiy bàkkaar, yedd leen fa kanam ñépp, ngir artu ñi ci des.    
1 Timothy 5 21  Léegi nag maa ngi lay dénk fa kanam Yàlla ak Kirist Yeesu ak malaaka yu tedd ya, nga sàmm loolu ma wax te bañ cee gënale walla di ci parlàqu. 
1 Timothy 5 22  Bul gaaw a teg loxo kenn, ba fal ko, di séddu noonu ci bàkkaari jaambur, waaye dëkkal cig sell.    
1 Timothy 5 23  Ba tey bul yemati ci ndox mu ñuul rekk, waaye nangay naan tuuti biiñ, ngir faj say metiti biir ak say jagadi yu bare.    
1 Timothy 5 24  Am na, ñu seeni bàkkaar fés ci kanamu ñépp, ba jiitu leen ca àtte ba; ñi seeni bàkkaar nëbbu nag, bés baa ngi leen di xaar. 
1 Timothy 5 25  Naka noonu it am na, ñu seen jëf yu rafet leer, te yi feeñul mënuñoo nekk kumpa ba fàww.
1 Timothy 6 1  Ñi nekk ci buumu njaam nag, nañu weg seeni sang wegeel gu mat sëkk; noonu kenn du am lu muy werante ci turu Yàlla mbaa ci sunu njàngale. 
1 Timothy 6 2  Ku am sang boo bokkal ngëm, bu looloo tax nga yab ko, waaye nga sax ci itteem, ndax kiy jariñu ci sa ñaq, aji gëm la, ku mat a bëgg. Jàngaleel loolu nag, di ko dénkaane. 
1 Timothy 6 3  Waaye su fi amee kuy jàngale leneen, ba jàppul ci kàddu yu wér yu Yeesu Kirist Boroom bi, te fonkul waaraate buy jur ragal Yàlla,
1 Timothy 6 4  kooku boroom tiitar la, bu xamul dara. Dafa wéradi, ba sóobu ci gëstuy neen ak i werante ciy araf yu dul jur lu dul ñeetaange, xuloo, xaste, ñaaw njort
1 Timothy 6 5  ak ŋaayoo; ñiy jëfee noonu nit ñu ñaaw xel lañu, ñu xamul genn dëgg te yaakaar ne, ragal Yàlla buntu wërsëg la.    
1 Timothy 6 6  Ba tey ragal Yàlla gu ànd ak doylu, wërsëg la. 
1 Timothy 6 7  Ndaxte indaalewunu fi dara, te dunu yóbbaale dara. 
1 Timothy 6 8  Kon su nu amee lekk ak koddaay, nanu ko doyloo. 
1 Timothy 6 9  Waaye ñiy sàkkoo barele, dinañu jànkoonte ak i nattu, ba dugg ci fiir, di xuus ci bëgg-bëggi neen yuy yóbbe ayib, tey sóob nit cig réer ak sànkute. 
1 Timothy 6 10  Ndaxte bëgge ci xaalis mooy ndeyu ñaawteef yu bare; am na ñu ko wut, ba moy ci yoonu ngëm, te seen xol di dagg ndax tiis yu bare.    
1 Timothy 6 11  Kon nag yaw waayu Yàlla ji, dawal loolu, te topp njub, ragal Yàlla, ngëm, mbëggeel, muñ ak lewet. 
1 Timothy 6 12  Góor-góorlul ci bëre bu baax bi, ba ub làmbi ngëm, te feddali sag téye ci dund gu dul jeex gi; ndaxte ci loolu la la Yàlla woo, te looloo waraloon it sa seede su rafet fa kanam mbooloo mu bare.    
1 Timothy 6 13  Noonu fi kanam Yàlla mi jagleel dund ci lépp, ak fi kanam Kirist Yeesu, mi seede woon seede su rafet fa kanam Poñsë Pilaat, maa ngi lay dénk lii: 
1 Timothy 6 14  sàmmal ndigal li, bañ a am gàkk mbaa ŋàññ, ba kera Yeesu Kirist sunu Boroom di feeñ ci ndamam, ca waxtu wa Yàlla dogal. 
1 Timothy 6 15  Moom kenn mooy Boroom bu tedd, di Buuru buur yi ak Kilifag kilifa yi. 
1 Timothy 6 16  Moom kenn a jagoo dund gu sax, dëkk ci biir leer gu kenn mënta jege; moom mi nit musul a gis te nit mënu koo gis. Moom kenn a yelloo teraanga ak màggaay ba fàww. Amiin.    
1 Timothy 6 17  Ñi barele alalu àddina nag, dénk leen ñu bañ a réy te bañ a wékk seen yaakaar ci koom-koom yi saxul fenn, waaye ñu wékk ko ci Yàlla, mi nuy may naataange ju mat, ngir nu man ciy bànneexu. 
1 Timothy 6 18  Dénk leen ñu def lu baax, te bare jëf yu rafet, ñu yéwén, bay sédd ñi amul, 
1 Timothy 6 19  di fàggu dencu ëllëg bu wér. Noonu dinañu feddali seen téye ci dund gu wóor gi.    
1 Timothy 6 20  Céy yaw Timote, sàmmal li la Yàlla dénk! Tanqamlul waxi neen yu àddina kese, te dëddu werantey ñi mbubboo xam-xam, fekk dañoo réer. 
1 Timothy 6 21  Am na ñu topp xam-xam boobu, waaye moy nañu ci yoonu ngëm. Na yiwu Yàlla ànd ak yéen.
2 Timothy 1 1  Man Pool, ndawul Yeesu Kirist ci coobareg Yàlla, ngir xamle dund gi nu Yàlla dig te féete ci Kirist Yeesu,
2 Timothy 1 2  maa ngi lay bind Timote, sama doomu diine ji ma bëgg. Na la Yàlla Baay bi ak Kirist Yeesu sunu Boroom may yiw, yërmande ak jàmm.    
2 Timothy 1 3  Fu ma tollu maa ngi lay boole ci samay ñaan, di ci sant Yàlla, mi may jaamu ci xel mu dal, ni ko samay maam daan defe. Guddi ak bëccëg, bu sama xel demee ci say rangooñ,
2 Timothy 1 4  ma bëgg laa gis, ba am mbég mu réy. 
2 Timothy 1 5  Maa ngi fàttaliku sa ngëm gu dëggu, gi nekkoon ci sa maam Lowis ak sa yaay Ënis, te mu wóor ma ne, sax na ci yaw it. 
2 Timothy 1 6  Looloo tax maa ngi lay fàttali, nga xambaat taal bi Yàlla taal ci yaw, di may gi mu la jagleel, bi ma la tegee samay loxo. 
2 Timothy 1 7  Ndaxte Xel mi nu Yàlla sol du ànd ak ragal, waaye day ànd ak kàttan, mbëggeel ak moom sa bopp.    
2 Timothy 1 8  Bul rus ci seedeel sunu Boroom, mbaa ci li ñu ma tëj ndax turam, waaye bokkal ak man tiis ci xamle xebaar bu baax bi, wéeru ci kàttanu Yàlla. 
2 Timothy 1 9  Moo nu musal te woo nu ci dund gu sell, ci lu ajuwul ci sunuy jëf, waaye ci dogalu boppam ak yiwam, wi nu Yàlla may ci Kirist Yeesu, ba àddina sosoogul. 
2 Timothy 1 10  Te léegi biral na ko ci feeñug sunu Musalkat Kirist Yeesu, mi nasaxal dee te feeñal dund ci xebaar bu baax bi, te muy dund gu sax. 
2 Timothy 1 11  Te Yàlla fal na ma ndaw ak jàngalekat, ngir may yégle xebaar bi; 
2 Timothy 1 12  looloo tax ma jànkoonte ak tiis yu mel nii. Waaye rusuma ci, ndaxte xam naa Ki ma wékk sama yaakaar, te wóor na ma ne, li ma ko dénk, man na koo denc ba bés ba.    
2 Timothy 1 13  Toppal ci tànki wax yu wér yi nga dégge ci man, jàpp ci ak ngëm ak mbëggeel, yi nu am ci sunu bokk ci Kirist Yeesu. 
2 Timothy 1 14  Te nga sàmm bu baax li la Yàlla dénk, wéeru ci Xel mu Sell, mi dëkk ci nun.    
2 Timothy 1 15  Xam nga ne, waa diiwaanu Asi gépp, won nañu ma gannaaw, ñu deme niki Fusel ak Ermosen. 
2 Timothy 1 16  Waaye Onesifor daa na faral di dëfël sama xol; na Boroom bi sotti yërmandeem ci këram. Rusul woon sax ci samay jéng, 
2 Timothy 1 17  waaye bi mu ñëwee dëkku Room, wut na ma fu ne, ba gis ma. 
2 Timothy 1 18  Na ko Boroom bi teeru ak yërmandeem ca bés ba. Umplewoo it coono yi mu daj, ngir dimbali ma ca dëkku Efes.
2 Timothy 2 1  Kon nag yaw sama doomu diine, doolewool yiw, wi ci Kirist Yeesu. 
2 Timothy 2 2  Te wax yi nga dégge ci man fi kanam seede yu bare, nanga leen jottali nit ñu takku, ngir ñoom it ñu man a jàngal ñeneen.
